kaṇḍapaḍavāi majjhē kaḍāhapalhatthiaṁ ṇiasu tissā || 28 || [ 25 ]

kāvī ṇīlā kāō lakkhē kālaṁ tamissammi |

kārākōṇū lēhā kāraṁ kaḍuammi kāhalī taruṇī || 26 ||

kāvī nīlavarṇā. kāō lakṣyam. vēdhyamityarthaḥ. anyē tu lakṣyaśabdēna yō yēna guṇēna lakṣyatē tamupamānabhūtaṁ padārthamāhuḥ. kālaṁ tamisram. kārā tathā kōṇū lēkhā. kāraṁ kaṭu. kāhalī taruṇī. yathā–

hayakāvikālalaharīi virahikārāi candakārāē |

mayaraddhayadhāṇukkō kāhalitaṇukōṇukāyamāhaṇaï || 29 || [ 26 ]

kārimamavi kittimaē kāsāraṁ sīsapattammi |

kāhārō parikhandhē kāsijjaṁ kāgathaladēsē || 27 ||

kārimaṁ kr̥trimam. kāsāraṁ sīsapatrakam. kāhārō parikhandhō. jalādivāhī karmakara ity arthaḥ. kāsijjaṁ kākasthalābhidhānō dēśaḥ. yathā–

kāsijjadēsaluṇṭhaṇakāhārāṇijjamāṇakaṇayāiṁ |

kāsāraṁ ca buhāṇaṁ akārimaṁ dēsi cālukka || 30 || [ 27 ]

kāyandī kāṇaddhī parihāsē kāhilō a gōvālē |

dhuttāsahaṇadhaṇūsuṁ kālayakāvaliakālavaṭṭhāiṁ || 28 ||

kāyandī tathā kāṇaddhī parihāsaḥ. kāhilō gōpālaḥ. kālaō dhūrtaḥ. ṭhaka ity arthaḥ. kāvaliō asahanaḥ. kālavaṭṭaṁ dhanuḥ. kālapr̥ṣṭhaśabdō yadi dhanurmātra vācī saṁskr̥tē rūḍhastadā saṁskr̥tabhava ēvāyam. anyathā tu dēśya ēva. asmābhi stvanēkadēśīṣvavigānēna darśanādayaṁ nibaddhaḥ. yathā–

caya hariaṁ majjha maṇaṁ kālaya kā kāhilāhi kāṇaddhī |

kāyandīi vi mayaṇō kāvaliō haṇaï kālavaṭṭhēṇa || 31 || [28]

kāṇatthēvō viralambukaṇē kāliñjaṇī a tāvicchē |

kāyandhuō a kāyañculō a kāmiñjulavihaṅgē || 29 ||

kāṇatthēvō viralāmbukaṇavr̥ṣṭiḥ. kāliñjaṇī tāpicchalatā. kēcitkāliñjaṇaṁ tāpicchamityāhuḥ. kālējjaṁ tāpicchakusumamityanyē. kāyandhuō tathā kāyañculō kāmiñjulākhyaḥ pakṣī. kāmiñjulaśabdō ’pi dēśya ēva bhaṅgayā nibaddhaḥ. ētē trayō ’pi jalapakṣiviśēṣavācakāḥ. yathā–

kāliñjaṇisāmalaghaṇakāṇatthēvē ruanti virahijaṇā |

rē kāyandhua kāyañculīi sahiō si kūjasu tubhaṁ tā || 32 || [ 29 ]

kāraṅkaḍō a pharusē kāyapiucchā ya kalakaṇṭhī |

kāmakisōrō a kharē kiṇṇaṁ sōhantaē kirō kōlē || 30 ||

kāraṅkaḍō. kapratyayē kāraṅkaḍaō paruṣaḥ. kāyapiucchā kōkilā. kāma kisōrō gardabhaḥ.

kiṇṇaṁ śōbhamānam. kirō sūkaraḥ. yathā–

sā kattha laliakiṇṇā kirō vva kāraṅkaḍaṅga kattha tumaṁ |

kaha kalakāyapiucchā kāmakisōrō kaḍujjhuṇī kattha || 33 || [ 30 ]

kimbōḍō khaliē kiṅkiaṁ ca dhavalammi kimpaō kivaṇē |

kiñjakkhō a sirīsē racchāē kilaṇikīlaṇiā || 31 ||

atra kira kilārthē. kiṇō kīsa praśnē. kiḍī sūkaraḥ. ētē śabdānuśāsanē siddhā iti nōktāḥ. kimbōḍō skhalitaḥ. kiṅkiaṁ dhavalam. kimpaō kr̥paṇaḥ. kiñjakkhō śirīṣaḥ. kilaṇī tathā kīlaṇiā rathyā. yathā–

kīlaṇikiñjakkhatalē vēsaṁ daṭṭhūṇa kiṅkiadugūlaṁ |

kimpaya tumaṁ muha ccia kilaṇīē bhamasi kimbōḍō || 34 || [ 31 ]

lahumacchē kindharakundharā ya sappammi kikkiṇḍī |

kahiē kilimmiaṁ taha lakkhārattammi kimirāyaṁ || 32 ||

kindharō tathā kundharō laghumatsyaḥ. kikkiṇḍī sarpaḥ. kilimmiaṁ kathitam. kimirāyaṁ lākṣāraktam. yas tu rudhirōdbhavakīṭamukhōdvāntatantuniṣpannaṁ tadvācī kimirāyaśabdaḥ kr̥mirāgaśabda-bhava ēva. atra ca. kilikiñcaï ramatē. iti dhātvādēśēṣūkta iti nōcyatē. yathā–

kikkiṇḍivēṇi kimirāyaṇivasaṇē kindharacchi tuha virahē |

tammaï thōvajalē kundharō vva sō ia kilimmēmi || 35 || [ 32 ]

kimiharavasaṇaṁ kōsēaē ṇavavahūi kīlakukulāō |

vēṇumayaücchupīḍaṇakaṇḍē kuṇḍaṁ ca kuḍḍamacchariē || 33 ||

kimiharavasaṇaṁ kauśēyaṁ vastram.

atha īkārāntakakārādiśabda ēka ēva || kīlā navavadhūḥ.

kukulā navavadhūrēva. kuṇḍaṁ vēṇumayaṁ jīrṇamikṣupīḍanakāṇḍam. yad āha— vēṇumaya mikṣupīḍanakāṇḍaṁ jīrṇa viduḥ kuṇḍaṁ || kuḍḍaṁ āścaryam. kēcitkōḍḍaṁ ity āhuḥ. tacca paraō ṭhiasañjōēity ādinā (1,174) ukāraōkāravinimayē siddham. yathā–

ua ṇāyarakīlāē kuṇḍaṁ pēcchantiāi parilhasaï |

kimiharavasaṇaṁ kuḍḍā chippantaṁ haliakukulāhiṁ || 36 || [ 33 ]

kukkhī kucchī kulhō a siālē pōṭṭalē kuṇṭī |

kumbhī sīmantāī kuddaṁ bahu mañjarī kuntī || 34 ||

kukkhī kukṣiḥ. kr̥kṣiśabdasya prākr̥tē ’kṣyādipāṭhācchatvē kucchīity ēva bhava tīti kukkhīśabdō dēśyaḥ. kulhō śrr̥gālaḥ. kuṇṭī pōṭṭalam. vastranibaddhaṁ dravyam. kumbhī sīmantālakādiḥ kēśaracanā. kuddaṁ prabhūtam. kuntī mañjarī. yathā–

ghēttuṁ sambalakuṇṭiṁ caïa piākumbhikuntikammāiṁ |

raṇṇammi kuddakulhē tuha riuṇō khāmakukkhiṇō janti || 37 || [ 34 ]

kuṭṭākumārikuṭṭayarīkōsaṭṭaïriāu caṇḍīē |

kuhiaṁ littammi kuhēḍō a gurēḍammi tīmaṇē kusaṇaṁ || 35 ||

kuṭṭā kumārī kuṭṭayarī kōsaṭṭaïriā ētē catvāraścaṇḍīvācakāḥ. atra kuḍō ghaṭa iti saṁskr̥takuṭaśabda-bhava ēvētyupēkṣitaḥ. kuhiaṁ lipram. kuhēḍō gurēṭakākhyō haritakaviśēṣaḥ. kusaṇaṁ tīmanam. yathā–

kōsaṭṭaïrīpiuṇō kumārisiharē sakuṭṭamacca halā |

kuṭṭayarivaïṁ sakusaṇabalīhi ghusiṇakuhiaṁ kuhēḍēhiṁ || 38 || [ 35 ]

hālammi kuntalō kukkusō tusē kuppaḍhō gharāyārē |

kuhaḍō khujjammi maṇōrahē kutattī a kuñcalaṁ maülē || 36 ||

kuntalō sātavāhanaḥ. kukkusō dhānyādituṣaḥ. kuppaḍhō gr̥hācāraḥ. samudācāra ity anyē. kuhaḍō kubjaḥ. kutattī manōrathaḥ. kuñcalaṁ mukulam. kumpalaṁ iti tu kuḍ‍malaśabdaprabhavamitīha nōktam. yathā–

ahariakuntalakuppaḍha adōsakukkusa kumāravāla ṇiva |

kuhaḍiasattukutattī disāsu jasakuñcalaṁ viāsēsu || 39 || [ 36 ]

mattammi kukkuḍō kundaō kisē kuṇḍiō vi gāmēsē |

kuṭṭāō cammayarē kuḍayakuḍaṅgā layāharaē || 37 ||

kukkuḍō mattaḥ. kundaō kr̥śaḥ. kuṇḍiō grāmādhipatiḥ. kuṭṭāō carmakāraḥ. kuḍayaṁ tathā kuḍaṅgaṁ latāgr̥ham. yathā–

kuṇḍiaputtō kuḍayā kuḍaṅgaē bhamaï tujjha aṇurattō |

kundayakuṭṭāaṁ piva ṇēcchasi jaṁ kukkuḍā si taṁ putti || 40 || [ 37 ]

gattāi kumbhiṇī kuntalī karōḍīi kuddaṇō rāsē |

ṇīvīē a kuūlaṁ kutthuhavatthaṁ ca kōsalaṁ cēa || 38 ||

kumbhiṇī jalagartaḥ. kuntalī karōṭikākhyaṁ parivēṣaṇōṣakaraṇam. kuddaṇō rā sakaḥ. kuūlaṁ kutthuhavatthaṁ kōsalaṁ ity ētē trayō ’pi nīvīvācakāḥ. kuūlaṁ parihitavastraprānta iti kēcit. yathā–

varaṇāhī kumbhiṇikuntalikammaṁ caïa khēlla kuddaṇayaṁ |

daḍhakōsalasahiāhiṁ kutthuhavatthaṁ daḍhēsu sukuūlē || 41 || [ 38 ]

kumbhillaṁ khaṇṇē kundīraṁ kōlhāhalaṁ ca bimbammi |

aṇaïṭṭhammi kuruccaṁ kumulī kulasantaī a cullīē || 39 ||

kumbhillaṁ khananīyam. kundīraṁ tathā kōlhāhalaṁ bimbyāḥ phalam. kuruccaṁ aniṣṭam. kumulī tathā kulasantaī cullī. yathā–

daṭṭhuṁ kundīrōṭṭhiṁ pahiā kōlhāhalāi cuṇṭanti |

kulasantaïmavi khaṇirō kuruccakumbhillakumuliō havaï || 42 || [ 39 ]

kurarī pasū milāṇē kummaṇakuṇṭārakurumāṇā |

pisuṇē kusumbhilō kōḍillō a kuḍillayaṁ kuḍilē || 40 ||

kurarī paśruḥ. kummaṇaṁ kuṇṭāraṁ kurumāṇaṁ trayamapi mlānārtham. atra kuppisō kañcuka iti kūrpāsaśabda-bhavaḥ. kusumbhilō tathā kōḍillō piśrunaḥ. kuḍillayaṁ kuṭilam. yathā–

akusumbhilā kuḍillayakēsī kōḍilla sā khu kurumāṇā |

kuṇṭārēi sahīu vi akummaṇō puṇa tumaṁ kurarī || 43 || [ 40 ]

kurucillaṁ gahaṇē kusumaṇṇaṁ ghusiṇē kuḍucciaṁ suraē |

gabbhiṇikulīrakanduiā kucchimaïkurucillakullariā || 41 |

kurucillaṁ grahaṇam. kusumaṇṇaṁ kuṅkumam. kuḍucciaṁ suratam. kucchimaī garbhiṇī. kurucillō kulīraḥ. kullariō kāndavikaḥ. yathā–

ō kurucillaï pahiō kurucillaṇihō kuḍucciassa kaē |

chaṇakusumaṇṇavilittaṁ kullariaṁ kucchimaïaṁ pi || 44 || [ 41 ]

kusumāliō a suṇṇamaṇē kurukuriaṁ ca raṇaraṇaē |

kulaphaṁsaṇō kulakalaṅkammi chuhāē a kuḍḍalēvaṇiā || 42 ||

kusumāliō śrūnyamanāḥ. kurukuriaṁ raṇaraṇakaḥ. kulaphaṁsaṇō kulakalaṅkaḥ. kuḍḍalēvaṇī sudhā. yathā–

mā kuḍḍalēvaṇīdhavalakuṭṭimē paravahuṁ ṇiēūṇa |

kusumālia kurukuriaṁ karēsu kulaphaṁsaṇō hōhī || 45 || [ 42 ]

kuṇḍiapēsaṇakuntīpōṭṭalayā bambhaviṭṭicaükōṇā |

kūlaṁ balapacchā kūḍō pāsē kūvalaṁ jaghaṇavasaṇē || 43 ||

kuṇḍiapēsaṇaṁ brāhmaṇaviṣṭiḥ. kuntīpōṭṭalayaṁ catuṣkōṇam.

kūlaṁ sainyasya paścādbhāgaḥ. kūḍō pāśaḥ. atra kūraṁ bhaktam itisaṁskr̥tasamatvā nnōktam. kūvalaṁ jaghanavasanam. yathā–

kuṇḍiapēsaṇakārīi kusumasarakūlakūvalavaīē |

kuntīpōṭṭalabhavaṇē ua paḍaï diō kaḍakkhakūḍammi || 46 || [ 43 ]

kūṇiamīsimaüliē gattākārammi kūsārō |

kēā rajjū kēlī asaī kēū a kandammi || 44 ||

kūṇiaṁ īṣanmukulitam. kūsārō gartākāraḥ.

kēā rajjuḥ. kēlī asatī. kēū kandaḥ. yathā–

kūsārakhalantapaō kēukaē pahia mā bhamasu kacchē |

jaṁ kēlīē kūṇiapēcchiakēāṇa paḍasi pāsēsu || 47 ||

atra kēddahaṁ kiyaditi śabda-bhavam. kēlāyaï samāracayatīti dhātvādēśa iti nōktau || [ 44 ]

kēāravāṇakōṭṭā kiṁsuaṇayarēsu kasiṇaē kōṇō |

kōlō gīvā kōppō avarāhē gēhakōṇaē kōṇṇō || 45 ||

kēārabāṇō palāśaḥ.

kōṭṭaṁ nagaram. kōṇō kr̥ṣṇavarṇaḥ. lakuṭa ity anyē. kōlō grīvā. kōppō aparādhaḥ. kōṇṇō gr̥hakōṇaḥ. yathā–

kēārabāṇaōḍayakōṇṇē kōṇāṇaṇā ṇamiakōlā |

maṇṇanti hariakōṭṭā tuha riuṇō kōppamappaṇayaṁ || 48 ||

atra kōō cakravāka iti kōkaśabda-bhavatvānnōktaḥ || [ 45 ]

kōccappaṁ aliahiē itthirahassammi kōjjappaṁ |

kōlīraṁ kuruvindē kōhallī tāviāē a || 46 ||

kōccappaṁ alīkahitam. kōjjappaṁ strīrahasyam. kōlīraṁ kuruvindam. kōhallī tāpikā. yathā–

daïammi sāvarāhē intē kōlīrarattaṇayaṇēaṁ |

kōhallipūvarayaṇā kōccappaṁ kuṇaï ahaha kōjjappaṁ || 49 || [ 46 ]

kōlambakōllarā piḍharē kōsayakōḍiā lahusarāvē |

kōṭṭimbō dōṇīē kōṭṭumbhaṁ karahaē tōē || 47 ||

kōlambō tathā kōllarō piṭharam. kōlambō gr̥hamityanyē. kōsayaṁ tathā kōḍiaṁ laghuśarāvaḥ. kōṭṭimbō drōṇī. kōṭṭumbhaṁ karāhataṁ vāri. yathā–

kōllarakōḍiavāṇia chaḍḍiakōlambakōsaō kīsa |

ṇivaḍasi kayakōṭṭumbhō ṇaīi kōṭṭimbaṭhiāmimaṁ ṇia vi || 50 || [ 47 ]

kōṭṭhammi kōtthalō kōmuī tahā puṇṇamāsīē |

bhēēṇa gāmabhōttā ya kōṇḍiō kōuā karīsaggī || 48 ||

kōtthalō kuśrūlaḥ. kōmuī sarvā pūrṇimā. śaradyēva paurṇamāsī kaumudī rūḍhā. iha tu yā kācitpūrṇimā sā kōmuī. ata ēva ca dēśī. yadāha. || kōmuimāha ca śāmbō yā kācitpaurṇamāsī syāt || kōṇḍiō bhēdēna grāmabhōktā. aikamatyaṁ grāmīṇānāmapāsya yō māyayā grāmaṁ bhunakti. kōuā karīṣāgniḥ. yathā–

kōtthalakammaṇiuttā kōṇḍiaputtassa diṇṇasaṅkēā |

saṇṇaï gāmaṇivahuā kōmuijōṇha pi kōuasaricchaṁ || 51 || [ 48 ]

kōṇḍhullū a ulūammi sivāē kōviā hōi |

kōlittaṁ ca alāammi kōilā kaṭṭhaaṅgārā || 49 ||

kōṇḍhullū ulūkaḥ. kōviā śrr̥gālī. kōlittaṁ ulmukam. kōilā kāṣṭhā ṅgārāḥ. yathā–

ṇisi ṇaïmintī kōviakōṇḍhullūṇaṁ ḍarēmi tassa kaha |

kōlittakōilēhiṁ ia lihiaṁ dūiāi kahaï vahū || 52 || [ 49 ]

kōlāhalō khagaruē sāvihajantummi kōṇḍaliā |

kōkkāsiaṁ viasiē āpūriaammi kōjjhariaṁ || 50 ||

kōlāhalō khagarutam. tumulamātravācī tvayaṁ saṁskr̥tasamaḥ. kōṇḍaliā śvāvi tsañjñaḥ prāṇiviśēṣaḥ. kōṇḍaliā kīṭa ity anyē. kōkkāsiaṁ vikasitam. kōjjha riaṁ āpūritam. yathā–

kōkkāsiacchi sāyaṁ jalamāṇintī ṇa kiṁ tumaṁ ḍarasi |

kōlāhalakōṇḍaliākōjjhariē ēttha tūhammi || 53 ||

atra kōhaṇḍīkōhalīśabdau kūṣmāṇḍīśabda-bhavau. kōkkaï vyāharati. kōā saï vikasati. kōṭṭumaï ramatē. ētē dhātvādēśēṣūktā iti nōktāḥ || [ 50 ]

kandō daḍhamattēsuṁ kaṇḍō dubbalavivaṇṇaphēṇēsu |

kaṇṭhō sūarasīmāsu kaḍō jhīṇē uvaraē a || 51 ||

kandō dr̥ḍhō mattaś ca. staraṇē 'pītyanyē. kaṇḍō durbalō vipannaḥ phēnaś cēti tryarthaḥ. kaṇṭhō sūkarō maryādā ca. kaḍō kṣīṇō mr̥taś ca || [ 51 ]

ṇicchiddē kaḍivatthē dāratthavivakkhaāsīsu |

gahaṇē vaṇē kaḍillaṁ kammantagharēsu kavvālaṁ || 52 ||

kaḍillaṁ niśrchidraṁ kaṭīvastraṁ dauvārikaḥ śatrurāśīrgahanaṁ vanaṁ cēti saptārtham. kavvālaṁ karmasthānaṁ gr̥haṁ cēti dvyartham. [ 52 ]

kaṅkālakarālēsu kalērō thēvōllavahalēsu |

bapphē a kasavvaṁ kagghāḍō ’gghāḍē kilāḍē a || 53 ||

kalērō kaṅkālaḥ karālaś ca. kasavvaṁ stōkamārdraṁ pracuraṁ bāṣpaś cēti caturartham kagghāḍō apāmārgaḥ kilāṭaś ca || [ 53 ]

śāliarakāgaüsahēsu karōḍō piḍharapaḍahēsu |

muhahariṇēsu a kamalō kalaō jjuṇatarusuvaṇṇayārēsu || 54 ||

karōḍō nālikēraṁ kākō vr̥ṣabhaś cēti tryarthaḥ. kamalō piṭharaḥ paṭahō mukhaṁ hari ṇaś cēti caturarthaḥ. kalaō arjunavr̥kṣaḥ suvarṇakāraś cēti dvyarthaḥ || [ 54 ]

bhikkhāpattaasōēsu karaṅkaṁ vagghalaṇṭṭāsu |

savalē vi a karaḍō kamaḍhō manthaṇipiḍharahaladharamuhēsu || 55 ||

karaṅkaṁ bhikṣāpātramaśōkavr̥kṣaś cēti dvyartham. karaḍō vyāghrō laṭvā karburaścēti tryarthaḥ. kākādivācī tu karaḍō karaṭaśabda-bhava ēva. laṭbāyāṁ tu liṅgapariṇāmē karaḍā. kamaḍhō dadhikalaśī piṭharaṁ halabhr̥nmukhaṁ cēti caturarthaḥ. kacchapē bhikṣu bhājanē da ityē ca kamaṭhaśabda-bhava ēva || [ 55 ]

mūlayamusalēsu kaḍantaṁ kusumuccayaïsūsu kaṇaō a |

gavviaṇaülasahīsuṁ kaliō kaüaṁ pahāṇacinghēsu || 56 ||

kaḍantaṁ mūlakaśākaṁ musalaṁ ca. kaṇaō kusumāvacaya iṣuś ca. kaliō garvitō nakulaḥ sakhī cēti tryarthaḥ. sakhyāṁ liṅgapariṇāmē kaliā. jñātārthas tu kali taśabda-bhava ēva. kaüaṁ pradhānaṁ cihnaṁ ca. atra kammaï kṣuraṁ karōti bhuṅktē cēti dhātvādēśēṣūktam itinōktam || [ 56 ]

cañcūttaṁsēsuṁ kaṇṇōllī ghaṇṭajhasaēsu kaḍuālō |

allayakayacittiakaṇaïṇṇēsuṁ kaṇaïaṁ cēa || 57 ||

kaṇṇōllī cañcuravataṁsaś ca. kaḍuālō ghaṇṭā laghumatsyaś ca. jhaṣaśabdāddhrasvārthē kapratyayē jhaṣaka iti rūpam. kaṇaïaṁ ārdraṁ kr̥taṁ citritaṁ kaṇākīrṇa cēti caturartham || [ 57 ]

pāḍalipasiddhaēsuṁ kalayandī kāhalō miuṭhagēsu |

kāyakalantaramēhēsu kāliā kāyalō piē kāē || 58 ||

kalayandī pāṭalā prasiddhaś ca. kēcitpāṭalāyāṁ kaṇayandītyāhuḥ. atra kāhī ity atītē bhaviṣyati ca pratyayē kr̥gō rūpam itinōktam. kāhalō mr̥duṣṭhakaś ca. kāta ravācī tu kātaraśabda-bhava ēva. kāliā śarīraṁ kālāntaraṁ mēghaś cēti tryarthā. kāyalō priyaḥ kākaś ca. kēcitpriyē kāyarōity āhuḥ || [ 58 ]

vayagaraṇatāviāsuṁ kāhallī taṇughaṇēsu kālimbō |

kāsiakiṇhā saṇhē vatthē taha sēavaṇṇammi || 59 ||

kāhallī vyayārtha dhānyādi tavaṇīti prasiddhamapūpādipacanabhāṇḍaṁ ca. kālimbō śarīraṁ mēghaś ca. kāsiaṁ tathā kiṇhaṁ sūkṣmavastraṁ śvētavarṇaṁ cēti dvāvapi dvyarthau || [ 59 ]

kiviḍī pāsaduvārē gharapacchimaaṅgaṇē cēa |

kiviḍaṁ taha ṇiddiṭṭhaṁ dhaṇṇakhalē tattha jāē a || 60 ||

kiviḍī pārśvadvāraṁ gr̥hapaścimāṅgaṇaṁ cēti dvyarthā. kiviḍaṁ dhānyakhalaṁ tatra dhānyakhalē yacca jātam || [ 60 ]

kaṇṇōvagaṇṇiāē kōūhalaē a kiriiriā |

kullō gīvāi tahā asamatthē chiṇṇapucchē a || 61 ||

kiriiriā karṇōpakarṇikā kautūhalaṁ ca. kullō grīvā asamarthaśrchinnapucchaś cēti tryarthaḥ || [ 61 ]

hariāṇugamē hariacchaḍḍavaē taha ya kuḍhakūvā |

kuhiṇī kuppararacchāsu kumbhilō cōrapisuṇēsu || 62 ||

kuḍhō tathā kūvō hr̥tānugamanaṁ hr̥tatyājakaś cēti dvāvapi dvyarthau. kuhiṇī kūrparō rathyā ca. kumbhilō cauraḥ piśrunaś ca || [ 62 ]

cullīē lahubhaṇḍē a kuṇḍhayaṁ kullaḍaṁ cēa |

adayaṇiuṇēsu kuruḍō kurulō puṇa kuḍilakēsē vi || 63 ||

kuṇḍhayaṁ tathā kullaḍaṁ cullī laghubhāṇḍaṁ cēti dvāv api dvyarthau. kuruḍō nirdayō nipuṇaś ca. kurulō punaradayanipuṇayōḥ kuṭilakēśē ’pīti tryarthaḥ || [ 63 ]

kīlāghāē samuācārē ṇammē a kupparaṁ bhaṇiaṁ |

chiddakuḍītuḍiēsu kuḍicchaṁ kōṭṭī du dōhakhalaṇāsu || 64 ||

kupparaṁ kīlāghātaḥ samudācārō narma cēti tryartham. kīlā surata uraḥprahaṇana viśēṣaḥ. kuḍicchaṁ vr̥tivivaraṁ kuṭī truṭitaṁ cēti tryartham. kōṭṭī dōhō viṣamāskha lanā ca || [ 64 ]

kōsō kōsumbhajalahisu kōliō tantuvāyalūāsu |

ucchuṇivīlaṇajantammi kōlhuō taha siālammi || 65 ||

kōsō kusumbharaktavastraṁ jaladhiś ca. kōliō tantuvāyō jālakārakr̥miś ca. kōlhuō ikṣunipīḍanayantraṁ śrr̥gālaś ca || [ 65 ]

khaḍḍā khāṇī khallā cammē khaḍḍaṁ ca maṁsummi |

khaṇaṁ khattaṁ khāē tilapiṇḍīē khalī cēa || 66 ||

khaḍḍā khāniḥ. parvatakhātamityanyē. khallā carma. khaḍḍaṁ śmaśru. khaṇṇaṁ tathā khattaṁ khātam. khalī tilapiṇḍikā. yathā–

khaḍḍā gharēsu khattaṁ vappē khaṇṇaṁ ca vāsabhavaṇammi |

khalibhōaṇāṇa khallambarāṇa tuha vēriāṇa dhī khaḍḍaṁ || 54 || [ 66 ]

khaṭṭaṁ kaḍhiāi khaḍaṁ tiṇammi khaddhakhariā ya bhuttammi |

khavaō khandhē asaīi khaṇḍaī khaḍḍiō mattē || 67 ||

khaṭṭaṁ tīmanam. khaḍaṁ tr̥ṇam. khaddhaṁ tathā khariaṁ bhuktam. khaddhaṁ pracurārthē 'pi lakṣyēṣu dr̥śyatē. khavaō skandhaḥ. khaṇḍaī asatī. khaḍḍiō mattaḥ. khalagaṇḍiō matta ity anyē. yathā–

khaṇḍaï taïā jantī ṇaccirakhavayā ṇa dēsi gharakiḍiaṁ |

khariakhaḍakhaḍḍiavasahakhaddhaṁ khaṭṭaṁ ṇiēsi kiṁ iṇhiṁ || 55 || [ 67 ]

khaḍuā muttā khaṇusā maṇadukkhē khañjarō vi sukkadumē |

khaṭṭaṅgaṁ chāyā khavvullaṁ vayaṇammi khaṇṇuō kīlē || 68 ||

khaḍuā mauktikāni. khaṇusā manōduḥkham. khañjarō śruṣkadrumaḥ. khaṭṭaṅgaṁ chāyā. khavvullaṁ mukham. khaṇṇuō kīlakaḥ. yathā–

dukkhavvullē kā tuha khaṇusā khaḍuāvaliṁ ṇa jaṁ lahasi |

khaṇṇuabhūē sahi khañjarammi kiṁ hōi khaṭṭaṅgaṁ || 56 || [ 68 ]

khaccallō ricchē khapparō vi lukkhē uḍummi khajjōō |

khaccōlakhañjaṇā vagghakaddamā khaggiō vi gāmēsē || 61 ||

khaccallō acchabhallaḥ. khapparō rūkṣaḥ. khappurōity anyē. khajjōō nakṣatram. khaccōlō vyāghraḥ. khañjaṇō kardamaḥ. khañjarīṭavācī tu saṁskr̥tabhava ēva. khaggi ō grāmēśaḥ. yathā–

khaccallā khaccōlā khañjaṇavisamā mahī jahiṁ gāmē |

khapparakhaggiadutthē mā vasa tassiṁ sukhajjōa || 57 || [ 69 ]

khaṭṭikkō sūṇavaïmmi khallirī khullirī a saṅkēē |

thūlēndhaṇaaggīē khandhaggī khōḍapajjālī || 70 ||

khaṭṭikkō saunikaḥ. khallirī tathā khullirī saṅkētaḥ. khandhaggī tathā khōḍapajjā lī sthūlēndhanāgniḥ. yathā–

guṇakhallirī taē khulliriṁ aṇintēṇa kammakhaṭṭikka |

sā visaï virahakhandhaggipīḍiā khōḍapajjāliṁ || 58 || [ 70 ]

lahubārammi khaḍakkī taha khavaḍiakhuṇḍayā khaliē |

bāhummi khandhayaṭṭhī a khandhamaṁsō a khalaïaṁ rittē || 71 ||

khaḍakkī laghudvāram. atra khasiō khacita iti khacitaśabda-bhavaḥ. khaḍḍaï mr̥drātīti dhātvādēśēṣūkta ity ētau nōktau. khavaḍiaṁ tathā khuṇḍayaṁ skhalitam. khuḍiaṁ khaṇḍitam ititu khaṇḍitaśabda-bhavam. khandhayaṭṭhī tathā khandhamaṁsō bāhuḥ. khalaïaṁ riktam. yathā–

sā laliakhandhayaṭṭhī tamākhuṇḍayalōakhalaïē maggē |

sahidiṇṇakhandhamaṁsā akhavaḍiamahisāriā khaḍakkīō || 59 || [ 71 ]

tarumakkaḍē khaḍahaḍī khandhīdhārō a uṇhajaladhārā |

khaḍaïakhavaliakharahiasaddā saṅkuciakuviapōttēsu || 72 ||

khaḍahaḍī tarumarkaṭaḥ. khandhīdhārō atyuṣṇajaladhārā. khaḍaïō saṅkucitaḥ. khavaliō kupitaḥ. kharahiō pautraḥ. yathā–

ua vihi kharahiaṇandaṇaüjjāṇē khaḍahaḍī khaḍaïō vi |

sīālōaṇakhandhīdhāraṁ daṭṭūṇa khavaliō tujjha || 60 ||

atra khaüraï kṣubhyatīti dhātvādēśēṣūktam itinōktam || [ 72 ]

khārayakhāiakhāramphiḍīu taha maülaparihagōhāsu |

khāḍaïaṁ paḍiphaliammi khikkhirī ḍumbacindhalaṭṭhīē || 73 ||

khārayaṁ mukulam. khāiā parikhā. khāramphiḍī gōdhā. khāḍaïaṁ pratiphalitam. khikkhirī ḍumbādīnāṁ sparśaparihārārthaṁ cihnayaṣṭiḥ. yathā–

khāialaṅghaṇa khārayamuhiā khikkhirikarā tuhārivahū |

khāḍaïaṇiaravēsu vi ḍariā khāramphiḍi vva lukkēi || 61 || [ 73 ]

khijjiakhiṅkhiṇikhikkhiṇḍā ya uvālambhabhasuakikkiṇḍā |

kuḍilahutuṭṭēsuṁ khullakhuḍḍakhuṭṭā cahuṭṭaē khuttaṁ || 74 ||

khijjiaṁ upālambhaḥ. khiṅkhiṇī śrr̥gālī. khikkhiṇḍō kr̥kalāsaḥ. atra khiraï kṣaratīti dhātvādēśēṣūkta iti nōktaḥ. khullaṁ kuṭī. khuḍḍaṁ laghu. khuṭṭaṁ truṭitam. khuttaṁ nimagnam. yathā–

khikkhiṇḍō vva tayā tumamuggīvō khiṅkhiṇīi va bhamēsi |

kiṁ ajja khuḍḍakhullē khijjēsi vihiṁ akhuṭṭaduhakhuttō || 62 || [ 74 ]

khuṇṇaṁ maḍhiē khumpā vuṭṭhittāṇammi khuḍḍiaṁ suraē |

khuluhō gupphē khuvaō gaṇḍuasamakaṇṭakillatiṇē || 75 ||

khuṇṇaṁ parivēṣṭitam. khumpā tr̥ṇādimayaṁ vr̥ṣṭinivāraṇam. khuḍḍiaṁ suratam. khuluhō gulphaḥ. khuvaō gaṇḍutsañjñatr̥ṇasadr̥śaṁ kaṇṭakitr̥ṇam. yathā–

khumpākhuṇṇataṇūō kharakhuvayapphāḍiantakhuluhāō |

vāsārattē kulaḍāu khuḍḍiatthaṁ ahisaranti || 63 ||

atra. khuppaï majjati. khuṭṭaï khuḍaï tuḍati. ētē dhātvādēśēṣūktā iti nōktāḥ. [ 75 ]

khuṅkhuṇikhuṅkhuṇayakhuṇukkhuḍiāō racchaṇakkasiraghāṇā |

paṇayapakōvē khuruḍukkhuḍī tahā khēlliaṁ hasiē || 76 ||

khuṅkhuṇī rathyā. khuṅkhuṇaō ghrāṇasirā. khuṇukkhuḍiā ghrāṇam. khuruḍukkhuḍī praṇayakōpaḥ. khēlliaṁ hasitam. yathā–

khuruḍukkhuḍiapaṇatthīpayaghāyacchuṭṭakhuṅkhuṇō bhaṭṭō |

khuṅkhuṇiāi khuṇukkhuḍimua dhōantō jaṇēṇa khēlliaï || 64 || [ 76 ]

khēālū asahē khōṭṭī dāsī danturammi khōsalaō |

khallaṁ vaïvivararaīsu vāmakararāsahēsu khavvakhavā || 77 ||

khēālū niḥsahaḥ. asahana ity anyē. atra khēḍḍaï ramatē dhātvādēśēṣūkta iti nōktaḥ. khōṭṭī dāsī. khōsalaō danturaḥ. yathā–

rē khēālua khōsala imāṇa khōṭṭīṇa majjhamāvaḍiō |

chuṭṭissasi kaha va tumaṁ akuṭṭiō ṭakkarāhi phuḍaṁ || 65 ||

khallaṁ vr̥tivivaraṁ vilāsaś ca. khavvō tathā khavō vāmakarō rāsabhaś cēti dvārvā dvyarthau || [ 77 ]

khaṇḍaṁ sirasurabhaṇḍēsu khaṇḍiō māgahāṇivārēsu |

kharathaüḍēsu kharullaṁ jiṇṇōvāladdhaēsu khajjiayaṁ || 78 ||

khaṇḍaṁ muṇḍaṁ madyabhāṇḍaṁ cēti dvyartham. khaṇḍiō māgadhō ’nivāraś ca. kharullaṁ kaṭhinaṁ sthapuṭaṁ ca. khajjiaṁ jīrṇamupālabdhaṁ ca || [ 78 ]

raṇamaṇaduhēsu khammakkhamō kharaḍiaṁ ca lukkhabhaggēsu |

khallaïaṁ saṅkuiamuiēsu khittayamaṇatthadittēsu || 79 ||

khammakkhamō saṅgrāmō manōduḥkhaṁ ca. manōduḥkhaviśēṣō ’nuśayaniḥ śvasitamityanyē kharaḍiaṁ rūkṣaṁ bhagnaṁ ca. khallaïaṁ saṅkucitaṁ prahr̥ṣṭaṁ ca. khittayaṁ anarthō dīptaṁ ca. dīptaṁ prajvālanamityarthaḥ || [ 79 ]

khōḍō sīmākaṭṭhē dhammiaē khañjaē cēa |

khōlō lahugaddahaē vatthassa ya ēgadēsammi || 80 ||

khōḍō sīmākāṣṭhaṁ dhārmikaḥ khañjaś cēti tryarthaḥ. khōlō laghugardabhō vastraikadēśaś ca || [ 80 ]

gañjō gallē gaḍḍī sayaḍē gajjō javē gaḍhō duggē |

gaḍḍhaṁ sayaṇē galiaṁ sumariamakkhavalaē gaṇēttī a || 81 ||

gañjō gallaḥ. gaḍḍī gantrī. gajjō javaḥ. gaḍhō durgam. gaḍḍhaṁ śayyā. galiaṁ smr̥tam. gaṇēttī akṣamālā. yathā–

mayaṇagaḍhaṁ gajjassa vi gañjaṁ gaḍḍhammi gaḍḍicakkakaḍiṁ |

galiaṁ galiuṁ bhikkhū gaṇiagaṇēttī vi mucchēi || 66 || [ 81 ]

gahaṇaṁ ajalaṭṭhāṇē gaṇḍīrī ucchukhaṇḍammi |

gattāḍī taha gāṇī gavāyaṇī kaḍujhuṇimmi gaddabbhō || 82 ||

gahaṇaṁ nirjalasthānam. gaṇḍīrī ikṣukhaṇḍam. gattāḍī tathā gāṇī gavādanī. mattāḍī gāyikēti gōpālaḥ . gaddabbhō kaṭughvaniḥ. yathā–

gaddabbhasaddakarahōciammi gahaṇammi dhavala mā vacca |

tattha ṇa duvvāgāṇī dūrē gaṇḍīrigattāḍī || 67 || [ 82 ]

gandhiagaddiagaddahasaddā duggandhadariakumuēsu |

gandīṇī cakkhuyagaṇakīlā gañjillagāḍiā vihurē || 83 ||

gandhiō durgandhaḥ. gaddiō garvitaḥ. gaddahaṁ kumudam. gandīṇī cakṣuḥsthaganakrīḍā. gañjillō tathā gāḍiō vidhuraḥ. yathā–

gandhia gaddia uiē gaddahaṇāhammi kāmagañjillō |

bhamia kimimāi gōsē karasi virahagāḍiāi gandīṇiṁ || 68 || [ 83 ]

gaḍḍurigāmēṇīō chagalīē gañchaō varuḍē |

gahaṇī taha bandīē gaharō diddhē dhaṇummi gaṇḍīvaṁ || 84 ||

gaḍḍarī tathā gāmēṇī chāgī. gañchaō varuḍaḥ. gahaṇī haṭhahr̥tā strī. gaharō gr̥dhraḥ. gaṇḍīvaṁ dhanuḥ. yathā–

gañcha vva dalia vaṁsaṁ gahaṇiṁ gāmēṇiaṁ ca tāḍanti |

dhī gaḍḍaribhōaṇayā pāvā gaṇḍīviṇō gaharaghōrā || 69 || [ 84 ]

gahiagavattā vaṅkiaghāsā gahiā ya kammamāṇāē |

ṇāsāē gandhalayā ya gaḍayaḍī vajjaṇigghōsē || 85||

gahiaṁ vakritam. gavattaṁ ghāsaḥ. gahiā kāmyamānā strī. atra gahilagagga raśabdau grahilagadradaśabda-bhavau. gañjiō kalyapāla iti gāñjikaśabda-bhavaḥ. gañjā hi surāgr̥hamucyatē. iti nōktāḥ. gandhalayā nāsā. gaḍayaḍī vajranirghōṣaḥ. yathā–

mēhammi gaḍayaḍantē agahiacittaṁ viṇā gahiajuvaïṁ |

siṅghaï gandhalayāē kō ṇu gavattaṁ va mālaīdāmaṁ || 70 || [ 85 ]

gōṭṭhīraē gaṇasamō gallapphōḍō ḍamaruammi |

gahakallōlō rāhū vivāhagaṇaē gaṇāyamahō || 86 ||

gaṇasamō gōṣṭhīrataḥ. gallapphōḍō ḍamarukaḥ. atra. gandhuttamā surēti saṁskr̥ tabhavaḥ. gaṇṭhicchēō granthicchēdaka iti granthicchēdaśabda-bhava iti nōktau. gahaka llōlō rāhuḥ. gaṇāyamahō vivāhagaṇakaḥ|| yathā–

gaṇasama gallapphōḍaṁ muhēṇa vāēsi kiṁ gaṇāyamaha |

gahagaṇavivarīagaïṁ gahakallōlaṁ ṇayā ṇēsi|| 71 | [ 86 ]

gaṇaṇāiā ya caṇḍii galalthaliaṁ galatthiaē |

gayasāulō virattē gandhāpisāō a gandhiaē|| 87||

gaṇaṇāiā caṇḍā. galatthaliō kṣiptaḥ. galatthiaṁ iti tu dhātvādēśēṣu kṣipērdhātōḥ siddhamityanēnārthanirdēśaḥ kr̥taḥ. gayasāulō viraktaḥ. kēcit gayasā ullō virakta ity āhuḥ. tatra sāullō anurāgō vakṣyatē. sa gatō yasya sa gayasā ulla ity ēva siddham. gandhāpisāō gāndhikaḥ|| yathā–

gaṇaṇāiāi bhattōsavammi ṇa samāgaü tti vēsāē |

gayasāulacittāē gandhāpisāō galatthaliō|| 72|| [ 87 ]

gayaṇaraī mēhē gajjaṇasaddō hariṇavarāṇaravammi |

gāgējjaṁ gējjaṁ manthiammi ṇavapariṇiāi gāgējjā || 88 ||

gayaṇaraī mēghaḥ. gajjaṇasaddō mr̥gavāraṇadhvaniḥ. gāgējjaṁ tathā gējjaṁ mathitam. gāgējjā navapariṇītā. yathā–

gāgējjavāvaḍā gāgējjā gējjāravaṁ miuṁ kuṇaï |

gayaṇaraïgajjigahiraṁ gajjaṇasaddaṁ suṇāntiā païṇō|| 73|| [ 88 ]

gāhammi gāhulī gāyarigōā gaggarīē a |

gāmapahāṇē gāmaṇigāmaüḍaggāmagōhagōhā ya || 89 ||

gāhulī krūrajalacaraḥ. gāyarī tathā gōā gargarī. gaggarī śabdō ’pi kēṣāñciddēśyaḥ. asmābhis tu gargarīśabda-bhavatvānnōktaḥ. yadi bhavati tadā paryāyabhaṅgayā darśitō 'sti. gāmaṇī gāmaüḍō gāmagōhō gōhō ētē catvārō ’pi grāmapradhānārthāḥ. gōhō bhaṭa ity anyē. puruṣa ity ēkē. gāmaṇisuaśabdō ’pi grāmapradhānavācītyanyē. yathā–

gāmaṇisuēṇa kēṇa vi gōhasuā bhaggagāyarī kahaï |

gāmaüḍagāmagōhaghariṇīṇa gāhulihayaṁ gōaṁ|| 74|| [ 89 ]

gāmahaṇagāmarōḍā gāmaṭṭhāṇachalagāmabhōīsu |

gumphō kārā gummī icchā guṇṭhī a ṇīraṅgī || 90 ||

gāmahaṇaṁ grāmasthānam. gāmarōḍō chalēna grāmabhōktā. antarbhēdaṁ kr̥tvā yō māyayā grāmaṁ bhunakti. gumphō guptiḥ. gummī icchā. guṇṭhī nīraṅgī. yathā–

taïā taṁ kayaguṇṭhiṁ gāmahaṇē suhaya gāmarōḍavahuṁ |

uvabhuñjati gummīē iṇiṁha lajjēsi kiṁ gumphē|| 75|| [ 90 ]

gumphī a sayavaīē gulaṁ guḍōladdhiā ya cumbiaē |

mutthasamutthammi tiṇē guṇḍaṁ turayāhamē guṇṭhō || 91 ||

gumphī śatapadī. gulaṁ tathā guḍōladdhiā cumbanam. guṇḍaṁ mustōdbhavaṁ lacakākhyaṁ tr̥ṇam. guṇṭhō adhamahayaḥ. yathā.

gumphisamāē jīē rattō guṇṭhu vva guṇḍiṇimahīē |

tīē ccia kuṇasu gulaṁ majjha guḍōladdhiaṁ muñca || 76 || [ 91 ]

mūlōcchasabhāmiabhāsēsuṁ gummiagulucchagutthaṇḍā |

guñjōlliaṁ ca guḍadāviaṁ ca piṇḍīkayatthammi || 92||

gummiaṁ mūlōtsannam. gulucchaṁ bhramitam. gutthaṇḍō bhāsapakṣī. atra guluñchō guñcha iti saṁskr̥tasamaḥ. tathā guṇṭhaï uddhūlayati. gumaï bhramati. guñjaï hasati. gummaï muhyati. ētē dhātvādēśēṣūktā iti nōktāḥ. guñjēlliaṁ tathā guḍadāliaṁ piṇḍīkr̥tam. yathā–

guñjēlliaṇīsāsaṁ guḍadāliahaṇukaraṁ ca gutthaṇḍa |

virahagulucchaṁ taha gummiaṁ ca uḍḍia kahēsu maṁ tassa || 77 || [ 92]

guttaṇahāṇaṁ piujaladāṇē guluguñchiō vayantariē |

guphagumiō surahī gēṇḍagēṇṭhuā ya thaṇavatthagaṇṭhīē || 93 |

guttaṇahāṇaṁ pitr̥bhyō jalāñjalidānam. atra gujjhaharō rahasyabhēdīti guhyahara śabda-bhavaḥ. tathā. gulalaï cāṭu karōti. guñjullaï ullasati. gummaḍaï muhyati. ētē dhātvādēśēṣūktā iti nōktāḥ. guluguñchiaṁ vr̥tyantaritam. unnamitārthaṁ tu unnamērutkṣipērvādēśāsiddham. guphagumiaṁ sugandhi. gēṇḍaṁ tathā gēṇṭhuaṁ stanayōrupari vastragranthiḥ|| yathā–

guluguñchia mayaguphagumiaṅgō mahasi kimagēṇḍamimaṁ |

guttaṇhāṇakaē chuṭṭagēṇṭhuā jāi jaṁ sariamēsā|| 78|| [ 93]

gēṇṭhullaṁ gōvillaṁ kuppāsē gēṇihaaṁ ca thaṇasuttē |

kīlāi gēṇḍuī gējjalaṁ ca gēvējjaē vaṇē gōṇḍaṁ || 94 ||

gēṇṭhullaṁ tathā gōvillaṁ kañcukaḥ. gēṇihaaṁ uraḥ sūtram. gēṇḍuī krīḍā. gējjalaṁ graivēyakam. gōṇḍaṁ kānanam. yathā–

gēṇḍuigōṇḍē gōriṁ sagējjalaṁ pulayaphuṭṭagōvillaṁ |

ua daṭṭhuṁ raïtisiōē gēṇṭhullaṁ gēṇihaaṁ ca avaharaï || 79 || [ 94 ]

gōcchāgōṇṭhīgōṇḍīgōñjīō mañjarīē a |

gōlō sakkhī gōlhā bimbī gōlī a manthaṇiā || 95 ||

gōcchā gōṇṭhī gōṇḍī gōñjī ētē catvārō mañjarīvācakāḥ. gōlō sākṣī. gōlhā bimbī. gōlī manthanī. yathā–

gōṇḍī gaṇḍē gōcchā bhālē gōṇṭhī urē thaṇē gōñjī |

gōlīsamajalaphusiāu ēttha gōlhōṭṭhi kō gōlō || 80|| [ 95 ]

gōvī bālā gōsaṁ gōsaggaṁ gōvaraṁ karīsammi |

gōbhaddā gōaggā racchāē gōhuraṁ ca gōviṭṭhā || 96||

gōvī bālā. gōsaṁ prabhātam. gōsargaśabdō yadi saṁskr̥tē rūḍhastadā tadbhavō gōsaggaśabdaḥ. anyathā tu dēśī. paryāyabhaṅgayā tvihōpāttaḥ. gōvaraṁ karīṣam. gōmaddā tathā gōaggā rathyā. gōhuraṁ gōbiṣṭhā. yathā–

gōvaraṇōhurakajjē gōaggaṁ gōvi mā bha/?/ gōsē |

vippijjasi jaṁ tassiṁ kēṇa vi gōbhaddavasahēṇa || 81 || [ 96 ]

gōndīṇaṁ sihipittē, gō/?/ gōsabhūhammi |

ṇavayaṇajaḍēsu gōccayaṇōsalā gōviō ajampiraē || 97 ||

gōndīṇaṁ mayūrapittam. gōṇikkō gōsamūhaḥ. gōccaō prājanadaṇḍaḥ. gōsaṇṇō mūrkhaḥ. gōviō ajalpākaḥ. yathā–

gōsasa gōviabhisaṁ gōṇikkaṁ gōccaēṇa kiṁ haṇasi |

mōraṁ kaḍakkhamāṇiṁ gōndīṇapiaṁ ṇivārasu biḍāliṁ || 82 || [ 97 ]

gōaṇṭā gōcaraṇēpu yōalā duddhabikaïṇī |

gōāliāu pāusakīḍā yōramphiḍī gōhā || 98 ||

gōaṇṭā gōvaraṇāḥ. gōaṇṭō syalaśrr̥ṅgaṭa ity anyē. gōaṇṭagōkhurallaśabdau vr̥ddhatvavācakāviti tu /?/. gōaṇā dugdhavikrayakartrā. ava gōillō gōmāniti matōrillādēśasiddham. tathā gō/?/ /?/ tvaśabda-bhavatvā nnōktam. yadāha || gōyukhamupannēpanē ’pi syāt|| iti ( ilāyudhaḥ 5, 11) gōāliā prāvr̥pi kīṭaviśēṣaḥ. gōdāmphiḍī gōdhā. yathā|

rēllia gōaṇṭapayaṁ gōālipiē ghaṇammi varisantē |

ganttīsu gōalāsuṁ gōramphiḍi mā kuṇāsaṇiṇivāyaṁ|| 83|| [ 98 ]

ghummiamuē gayaṁ vaṇatalārabālamigaṇhāviē gaṇḍō |

gattaṁ īsāpaṅkēsu iccharayaṇīsu gandhōllī || 99 ||

gayaṁ ghūrṇitaṁ mr̥taṁ ca. gaṇḍō vanaṁ dāṇḍapāśikō laghumr̥gō nāpitaś cēti caturarthaḥ. samāhāratvādēkavacanam. gattaṁ īṣā paṅkaś ca. gandhōllī icchā rajanī ca || [ 99 ]

gandhēllī chāyāsarahāsu gahavaī a gāmiasasīsu |

gañjōlliamuddhusiaṁ hāsaṭṭhāṇē a aṅgamāliddhaṁ || 100 ||

gandhēllī chāyā madhumakṣikā ca. gahavaī grāmīṇaḥ śaśī ca. grahapatitvamāditya ēva rūḍhaṁ na śaśinīti nāyaṁ grahapatiśabdasamudbhavaḥ. gañjōlliaṁ rōmāñcitaṁ tathā hāsyasthānē ’ṅgasparśō yat giligilāviaṁ iti lōkē rūḍham itivdyartham || [ 100 ]

binduahamēsu gumpāgundāguñchāu dāḍhiāē vi |

guttī bandhaṇāicchāvayaṇalayāmaülimālāsu || 101 ||

gumpā tathā gundā bindāvadhamē cēti pratyēkaṁ vdyarthā. guñchā tu bindvadhamayōruttarō ṣṭaśmaśruṇi cēti tryarthā. guttī bandhanamicchā vacanaṁ latā śirōmālyaṁ cēti pañ‍cārthā || [ 101 ]

sējjāē sammūḍhammi gōviē taha ya guppantaṁ |

gumilaṁ mūḍhē gahaṇē pakkhāliāvusaēsuṁ ca || 102 ||

guppantaṁ śayanīyaṁ sammūḍhaṁ gōpitaṁ cēti tryartham. gumilaṁ mūḍhaṁ gahanaṁ praskhalitamā pūrṇaṁ cēti caturartham || [ 102 ]

busiāvilōḍa़iēsuṁ kaṇḍuathavaēsu taha guliā |

sañcaliakhaliavihāḍiapūriamūḍhēsu gummaïō || 103 ||

guliā busikā vilōḍitaṁ kandukaḥ stabakaś cēti caturarthā. gummaïō sañca litaḥ skhalitō vighaṭitaḥ pūritō mūḍhaś cēti pañcārthaḥ || [ 103 ]

paṅkajavēsuṁ gēḍḍaṁ gōgōdāṇaïsahīsu gōlā ya |

sīakkhiggīvāsuṁ gōrā gōṇō a sakkhiusahēsu || 104||

gēḍḍaṁ paṅkō yavaś ca. gōlā gaurgōdāvarī sāmānyēna nadī sakhī cēti caturarthā. gōrā lāṅgalapaddhatiścatturgrīvā cēti tryarthā. gōṇō sākṣī vr̥ṣabhaś ca. atra gōlā śabdaḥ saṁskr̥tasamō ’pi kavīnāṁ nātiprasiddha ity upāttaḥ. gōṇaśabdas tu gavi śabdā nuśāsanē sādhitō ’pi gōṇādiprapañcatvādasya prabandhasyēhōpāttaḥ|| [ 104 ]

ghaṇṇō uratthalē ghallō aṇurattē gharē ghaṅghō |

ghaḍighaḍiaghaḍā gōṭṭhī gharagōlīē gharōlī a || 105 ||

ghaṇṇō uraḥ. ghaṇṇō rakta ity anyē. ghallō anuraktaḥ. ghaṅghō gr̥ham. ghaḍī tathā ghaḍiaghaḍā gōṣṭī. gharōllī gr̥hagōlikā. yathā–

ghallassa ghaṅghavaïṇō ghasē laggāi kaha ghaḍīruiṇō |

ghaḍiaghaḍā ṇīsaṅkā bhamaï jamattā gharōli vva || 84 || [ 105 ]

gharabhōaṇē gharōlaṁ sadhammiṇīē gharillī a |

ghaṅghōrō hiṇḍaṇāē ghammōī gaṇḍuatiṇammi || 106 ||

gharōlaṁ gr̥habhōjanabhēdaḥ. gharillī patnī. ghaṅghōrō bhramaṇaśīlaḥ. ghammōī gaṇḍu tsañjñaṁ tr̥ṇam. yathā–

saha tīē hiṇḍa tumaṁ ghammōīsaddalāi ghaṅghōra |

bhuñjihisi gharōlē puṇa surasē disē gharillīē || 85 || [ 106 ]

jahaṇātthavatthabhēē ghaggharamājarirāyammi gharayandō |

ghaṇavāhī indē gharaghaṇṭō caḍaē a saüliā ghārī || 107 ||

ghaggharaṁ javanasthavastrabhēdaḥ. gharayandō ādarśaḥ. vaṇavāhī indraḥ. gharaghaṇṭō caṭakaḥ. ghārī śakunikākhyaḥ pakṣī. yathā–

ghaṇavāhidhaṇumaṇaharē kālē gharaghaṇṭaghārisaṅgharaṇē |

sayalakalāgharayandō kō jaṁ siḍhilantaghaggharā sarasi || 86 || [ 107 ]

pāyārammi a ghārō ghārantō ghēvarē cēa |

gāṇammi ghāyaṇō bhacchiē ghiaṁ khujjaē ghiṭṭō || 108 ||

ghārō prākāraḥ. ghārantō ghr̥tapūraḥ. ghāyaṇō gāyanaḥ. ghiaṁ bhartsitam. ghiṭṭō kubjaḥ |. yathā–

ghārantē bhikkhantō gēhaduvārē ghiō pariaṇēṇa |

ō ghiṭṭaghāyaṇō dhiṭṭhayāi ghārammi āruhaï || 87 ||

atra. ghisaï grasatē. iti dhātvādēśēṣūkta iti nōktaḥ || [ 108 ]

bhēkē ghugghurighurughuriṇō ghuttiaghusiṇiā gaviṭṭāmmi |

ghuṅghuruḍō ukkērē ghugghussusayaṁ sasaṅkabhaṇiammi || 109 ||

ghugghurī tathā ghurughurī maṇḍūkaḥ. ghuttiaṁ tathā ghusiṇiaṁ gavēṣitam. ghuṅghu ruḍō utkaraḥ. ghugghussusayaṁ sāśaṅkabhaṇitam. yathā–

pasariaghugghurighurughuriṇiravē sā ghuttiraha ghuṅghuruḍē |

tā ghusiṇasu dūi tumaṁ ia ghugghussusaïō cavaï kō vi || 88 ||

atra ghusiṇaṁ kuṅkumam itighusr̥ṇaśabda-bhavam. tathā. ghuṭṭaï pibati. ghulaï ghummaï ghūrṇatē. ghusalaï mathnāti. ētē dhātvādēśēṣūktā iti nōktāḥ|| [ 109 ]

kaṇṇōvaaṇiāē ghuṇaghuṇiā ghusirasāramavaṇhāṇē |

ghuṭṭaghuṇiaṁ girigaḍē ghugghucchaṇayaṁ ca khēammi || 110||

ghuṇaghuṇiā karṇōpakārṇikā. ghusirasāraṁ avasnānam. masūrādīnāṁ piṣṭam. ghuṭṭaghuṇiaṁ girērgaḍam. pr̥thuśilā. ghugghucchaṇayaṁ khēdaḥ. yathā–

tuha āgamaghuṇadhuṇiaṁ sōuṁ caïūṇa ghusirasārāiṁ |

ghuṭṭaghuṇiēsu ghugghucchaṇēṇa vaccanti riuvahuā || 89 ||

atra ghūō ulūka iti ghūkaśabda-bhavaḥ || [ 110 ]

ghōrī salahavisēsē ghōsālī sarayavallibhēāmmi |

ghaṭṭō kusumbharattē sariātūhammi vaṁsē a || 111 ||

ghōrī śalabhaviśēṣaḥ. atra ghōḍō aśva iti ghōṭaśabda-bhavaḥ. ghōsālī śaradudbhavō vallibhēdaḥ. yathā–

sirikumaravāla ṇaravaï tuha turayā ghōriṇō vva agaṇijjā |

kavalanti vēripatthivabalāi ghōsāliādalāiṁ va || 90 ||

atra. ghōlaï ghūrṇatē. iti dhātvādēśēṣūkta iti nōktaḥ.

ghaṭṭō kusumbharaktaṁ vastraṁ nadītīrthaṁ vēṇuś cēti tryarthaḥ || [ 111 ]

ghammōḍī majjhaṇahē masaē gāmaṇitiṇē cēa |

ghōrō ṇāsiagiddhēsu ghōliaṁ silayalē haḍhakaē a || 112 ||

ghammōḍī madhyāhnō maśakhō grāmaṇīsañjñaṁ tr̥ṇaṁ cēti tryarthā. atra ghattaï kṣipati gavēṣayati cēti dhātvādēśēṣūktam itinōktam. ghōrō nāśitō gr̥dhrapakṣī ca. ghōliaṁ śilātalaṁ haṭhakr̥taṁ ca || [ 112 ]

cattō takkū caṅgaṁ cāruṁ caḍacōṭṭiāu sihā |

caṭṭū a dāruhatthē cambhō cāsō a sīrasīmantē || 1 ||

cattō tarkuḥ. caṅgaṁ cāru. caḍō tathā cōṭṭī śikhā. caṭṭū dāruhastaḥ. cambhō tathā cāsō halasphāṭitabhūmirēkhā. yathā–

rē caṅgacōṭṭia caḍaṁ cōḍissaṁ caṭṭuēṇa ya haṇissaṁ |

cāsakkhamaṁ ghaḍakusiṁ ṇa hu cambhaṁ karaï cattamittakusī || 1 || [ 1 ]

cattharicahuṭṭacaṇḍikkā hāsaṇimaggarōsēsu |

candilacaükkacakkōḍā ṇāviacaccarāggibhēēsu || 2 ||

cattharī hāsaḥ. cahuṭṭaṁ nimagnam. caṇḍikkō rōṣaḥ. candilō nāpitaḥ. caṇḍila iti tu saṁskr̥tasamam. caükkaṁ catvaram. cakkōḍā agnibhēdaḥ. yathā–

tīi virahacakkōḍājaliō sō candilō sahi iāṇiṁ |

hiayacaükkē catvaricahuṭṭaṇakkhō vi kuṇaï caṇḍikkaṁ || 2 ||

castaricatuṣkaśabdau yēṣāṁ saṁskr̥tē ’pi sammatau tanmatē cattharicaükkaśabdau na dēśyau || [ 2 ]

pīṇācchiṇṇavigāṇēsu caṇḍilacaṇḍiacavēṇā |

juakarapuḍē cavēḍī tajā cakappā cuḍuppā ya || 3 ||

caṇḍilō pīnaḥ. caṇḍiō kr̥ttaḥ. cavēṇaṁ vacanīyam. cavēḍī śliṣṭaṁ karasampu ṭam. cavēḍī sampuṭamityanyē. cakappā tathā cuḍuppā tvak. cuḍuppaṁ tvagvidalana mityanyē. yathā–

caṇḍiacakappavasaṇā cuḍuppakandāsaṇāhuacavēṇā |

riuṇō acaṇḍilā tuha kuṇanti bhillāṇa vi cavēḍiṁ || 3 || [ 3 ]

caccikkacittalā maṇḍiammi kumuammi candōjjaṁ |

cakkhuḍḍaṇaṁ ca pēkkhaṇaē cañcapparamasaccammi || 4 ||

caccikkaṁ tathā cittalaṁ maṇḍitam. cittalaṁ ramaṇīyamityanyē. candōjjaṁ kumu dam. svārthē kē candōjjayaṁ. atra candimā candrikā. cavalā vidyut. iti candrikācapalāśabda-bhavau. cavaï kathayati. cayi śaknōti. cajjaï paśyati. cacchaï takṣṇōti. ityādayō dhātvādēśēṣūktā iti nōktāḥ. cakkhuḍḍaṇaṁ prēkṣaṇī yam. cañcapparaṁ asatyam. yathā–

cañcapparaṁ ṇa bhaṇimō kuṇēsi cakkhuḍḍaṇō kaḍakkhēhiṁ |

candujjayacaccikkā disāu mayaṇāhicittalakavōlē || 4 || [ 4 ]

mōrammi candaïllō caükkarō kattikēammi |

caḍiārō āḍōvē ahibhēē cakkulaṇḍā ya || 5 ||

candaïllō mayūraḥ. caükkarō kārttikēyaḥ. caḍiārō āṭōpaḥ. cakkulaṇḍā sarpaviśēṣaḥ. yathā–

gaṇavaïgajjiaṇaccantacaükkaracandaïllasaddēhiṁ |

taṭṭhagalacakkulaṇḍō ṇaccaï ruddō sacaḍiāraṁ || 5 || [ 5 ]

ṇāmammi carullēvaṁ cakkhaḍiaṁ jīviavvammi |

caṇḍaṭṭhiā ya khavaē ummīē cakkaṇāhayaṁ cēa || 6 ||

carullēvaṁ nāma. cakkhaḍiaṁ jīvitavyam. candaṭṭhiā bhujaśikharam. stabaka ity antē. yad āhuḥ || stabakaś candaṭṭhiāsañjñaḥ || iti. atra. cañcarīō bhramaraḥ. candasālā jālakr̥tā gr̥hōpari kuṭikā. iti cañcarīkacandraśālāśabda-bhavau. caccu ppaï arpayati. camaḍhaï bhuṅktē. cakkamaï bhramati. ityādayō dhātvādēśēṣūktā iti nōcyantē. cakkaṇāhayaṁ ūrmiḥ|| yathā–

ṇīsāsacakkaṇāhayatāviacandaṭṭhiāi tuha virahē |

kaṇṭhammi tīi vaṭṭaï cakkhaḍiaṁ tuha tahā carullēvaṁ || 6 || [ 6 ]

hālammi caüracindhō ṇāraṅgaphalammi cakkaṇabhayaṁ ca |

candavaḍāyā addhāvariaṅgī cakkhurakavaṇī lajjā || 7||

caüracindhō sātavāhanaḥ. cakkaṇabhayaṁ nāraṅgaphalam. candavaḍāyā ardhaprāvr̥tadēhā. cakkhurakkhaṇī lajjā. yathā–

daṭṭhūṇa tumaṁ cakkaṇabhayatthaṇī avaracaüracindhaṁ va |

tammaï candavaḍāyā muddhā vi hu mukkacakkhurakkhaṇiā || 7 ||

atra calaṇāuhō kukkuṭa iti caraṇāyudhaśabda-bhavaḥ|| [ 7 ]

caḍulātilayaṁ kañcaṇasaṅkāliālambirayaṇātilayammi |

saḍhataṇḍulasirabhūsāsu cāḍacāulayacālavāsā ya || 8 ||

caḍulātilayaṁ kāñcanaśrr̥ṅkhalālambiratnatilakam. caḍulā ratnatilakamityanyē. cāḍō māyāvī. cāulā taṇḍulāḥ. cālavāsō śirōbhūṣaṇabhēdaḥ. yathā–

jīē tujjha ṇihittaṁ caḍulātilayaṁ ca cālavāsō a |

taṁ cēa cāḍa aṇusara kiṁ cāulakhaṇḍalīi maē || 8 || [ 8 ]

gaṇṭhicchēayagimhāṇilēsu cāraṇayacāravāyā vi |

cillā saülīē civiḍaṇāsaē ciccaciccarayā || 9 ||

cāraṇaō granthicchēdakaḥ. kapratyayābhāvē cāraṇō. cāravāō grīṣmānilaḥ. cillā śakunikākhyaḥ pakṣī. ciccō tathā ciccarō cipiṭanāsaḥ. yathā–

ṇa hu mēllaï paharantō hī ciccaṁ ciccaraṁ ca cillaṁ ca |

ua mayaṇō māṇiṇi māṇagaṇṭhicāraṇayacāravāyasahō || 9 || [ 9 ]

bālammi cillacēḍā ciccaṁ ramaṇē huāsaṇē ciccī |

ciñciṇiciñcā ambiliāē taha ciñcaṇī gharaṭṭhīē || 10 ||

cillō tathā cēḍō bālaḥ. ciccaṁ ramaṇam. ciccī hutāśanaḥ. ciñciṇī tathā ciñcā amlikā. kaiścit ciñciṇiciñcāśabdaḥ samasta ēva amlikāvācakatvēna prōktaḥ. ciñcaṇī gharaṭṭikā|| yathā–

ciñcavaṇē ciñciṇiācaḍiē cēḍammi ciccaṭhiacillā |

ua dhāvaï jaṇaṇī caïa ciñcaṇīciccikammāiṁ || 10 || [ 10 ]

masayammi cillirī rōmasammi cimiṇō kuḍīi cirayā ya |

cikkhallō kaddamaē musalē cillūracēlumpā || 11 ||

cillirī maśakaḥ. cimiṇō rōmaśaḥ. cirayā kuṭī. cikkhallō kardamaḥ. cillūraṁ tathā cēlumpaṁ musalaṁ. yathā–

cikkhalliacirayāē cilliriḍasiā tuhāriṇō cimiṇā |

kaṇḍanti sayaṁ cillūraēṇa cēlumpapāṇitupallabalā || 11 ||

atra ciñcaï maṇḍayatīti dhātvādēśēṣūkta iti nōktaḥ|| [ 11 ]

ullē ciliccilaciliccīlā paritōsiammi cittaṭhiō |

cirihiṭṭī a ciṇōṭṭhī mahupaḍalē cittadāū a || 12 ||

ciliccilaṁ tathā ciliccīlaṁ ārdram. cittaṭhiō paritōṣitaḥ. cirihiṭṭī guñjā. ciṇōṭṭhīśabdō ’pi dēśyaḥ. paryāyabhaṅgayā tūpāttaḥ. cittadāū madhupaṭalam. kēcit. tiṇisammi cittadāū iti paṭhanti tiṇisaṁ ca vr̥ttaviśēṣamācakṣatē. asmābhis tu sāratadēśīdarśanēna tiṇisaśabdō madhupaṭalārthō vyākhyātaḥ. tatra yuktāyuktatvē bahudr̥śvānaḥ pramāṇam. yathā–

savarō sēaciliccilamaṁsuciliccīlamarivahuṁ tujjha |

cirihiṭṭilōaṇō mahaï cittadāuṁ ca cittaṭhiacittō || 12 || [ 12 ]

caṇḍātakammi cimphullaṇī ciricirāciriñcirā dhārā |

caliammi a ciñcaïō ṇiṇṇāsiayammi ciddaviō || 13 ||

cimphullaṇī strīṇāmarghōṁrukavastram. ciricirā tathā ciriñcirā jaladhārā. ciñcaïō calitaḥ. ciñcaïō maṇḍita iti tu maṇḍidhātvādēśē siddhaḥ. ciddaviō nirnāśitaḥ. yathā–

ghaṇajalaciriñcirāciddaviā pavasiavahūu ciñcaïā |

ṇayaṇaṁsuciricilōlliacimphullaṇiāu piahuttaṁ || 13||

atra ciñcillaï maṇḍayatīti dhātvādēśēṣūkta iti nōktaḥ || [ 13 ]

dahiē ciriḍḍihillaṁ cīhī mutthāsamutthatiṇē |

cīvaṭṭī bhallīē cukkō muṭṭhīi cujjamacchariē || 14 ||

ciriḍḍihillaṁ dadhi. cīhī mustōdbhavaṁ tr̥ṇam. cīvaṭṭī bhallī. cukkō muṣṭiḥ. cujjaṁ āścaryam. ōtsaṁyōgē. iti cōjjaṁ ity api. yathā–

sā hiṇḍirē taï ciriḍḍihillamatta ṇavacīhisamayammi |

daḍhacukkakāmacīvaṭṭitāḍiā jaṁ jiēi taṁ cujjaṁ || 14 || [ 14 ]

parisōsiammi cuñchō sasiṇēhē cuppacōpphuccā |

cullī silāi cuḍulī ukkā cuṇiō vidhāriaē || 15||

cuñchō pariśōṣitaḥ. cuppō tathā cōpphuccō sas‍nēhaḥ. cullī śilā. atra. cucchaṁ tuccham. iti tucchaśabda-bhavatvānnōktam. cuḍulī ulkā. cuṇiō vidhāritaḥ. yathā–

sundara taï cōpphuccā acuppavirahaggicuḍulicuñchā vi |

bāladharia vva cullī sā acchaï āsatantucuṇiappā || 15 || [ 15 ]

cuṇṇāsī dāsī cuñcuacuppalacumbhalā ya sēharaē |

cuṇṇāā ya kalāē chāgammi a cukkuḍaculuppā || 16 ||

cuṇṇāsī dāsī. cuñcuō tathā cuppalō tathā cumbhalō śēkharaḥ. cuṇṇaā kalā. cukkuḍō tathā culuppō chāgaḥ. yathā–

cuṇṇāsīē sacuṇṇaāē cuppalaculuppiduddhāiṁ |

rē jaḍacumbhalacukkuḍa appasu kiṁ cuñcuāiṇā majjha || 16 || [ 16 ]

atra cukkaï bhraśyatīti dhātvādēśēṣūktam itinōcyatē.

cuppālaō gavakkhē vatthē ṇavarattayammi cuppaliaṁ |

cullōḍaō vi jēṭṭhē cuṇṇappahayammi cuplaïō || 17||

cuppālaō gavākṣaḥ. cuppaliaṁ navaraktaṁ vastram. cullōḍaō jyēṣṭhaḥ. cuṇṇaïō cūrṇāhataḥ. cuṇṇiō rēṇuvicchurita iti tu cūrṇitaśabda-bhavaḥ. yathā–

cuppālayadārēṇaṁ ṇavacuppaliāi picchapaharantī |

ō cullōḍayajāyā cusaïā dēarēṇa phagguchaṇē || 17 || [ 17 ]

alasammi cuñcumālī cuñculipūrō a culuammi |

valayāvalithaṇasihavāmaṇaēsuṁ cūḍacūacōlā ya || 18 ||

cañcamālī alasaḥ. cuñculipūrō culukaḥ. atra culuculaï spandana iti dhātvādē śēṣūktam itinōktam. cūḍō valayāvalī. cūō stanaśikhā. cōlō vāmanaḥ. yathā–

tuha jalacuñculipūrō vi dullahō cuñcumāliṇō cōla |

maṇicūḍamaṇḍiā cārucūaā kāmiṇīu kiṁ mahasi || 18 || [ 18 ]

mālūratōttaṇahasiicōddasiā cōḍhacōttacōrāliā |

caccā ya hatthabimbē talappahārē a ṇāyavvā || 19 ||

cōḍhō bilvaḥ. cōttaṁ pratōdaḥ. cōralī śrāvaṇakr̥ṣṇacaturdaśī. yathā–

cōralipavittayachaṇē cōḍhadalēhiṁ taē harō mahiō |

mayaṇasaracōttaṇusā jaṁ tumamēsā ahisarēi || 19 ||

cōppaḍaï bhrakṣatīti dhātvādēśēṣūktamitīha nōktam.

caccā sthāsakaḥ prasr̥tahastāghātaś ca || [ 19 ]

caṇḍijjō khalakōvēsu capphalaṁ sēharē asaccē a |

kuṇḍalavaṭṭuladōlāphalayavisālēsu cakkalayaṁ || 20 ||

caṇḍijjō piśrunaḥ kōpaś ca. capphalaṁ śēkharaviśōṣō ’satyaṁ ca. sāmānyaśabdā api viśēṣē vartanta iti hi nyāyaḥ. cakkalaṁ kuṇḍalaṁ vartulaṁ dōlāphalakaṁ viśālaṁ cēti caturartham. atra caḍḍaï mr̥drāti bhuṅktē pinaṣṭi cēti dhātvādēśēṣūktamiti nōktam || [ 20 ]

cārō piālaguttīcchāsuṁ cikkāppataṇuadhārāsu |

cammamayavāribhaṇḍē taṇudhārādiṇamuhēsu a cirikkā || 21 ||

cārō piyālavr̥kṣō bandhanasthānamicchā cēti tryarthaḥ. cikkā alpaṁ vastuṁ tanudhārā cēti dvyarthā. cirikkā carmamayajalabhāṇḍaṁ tanudhārā pratyūṣaś cēti tryarthā || [ 21 ]

cindhālaṁ rammē uttamē a cullō sisummi dāsē a |

pāṇappabālamukkacchandāruivaïarēsu cuṇaō vi || 22 ||

cindhālaṁ ramyaṁ mukhyaṁ ca. cullō śiśurdāsaś ca. cuṇaō caṇḍālō ’lpō bālō muktaśrchandō ’rōcakō vyatikaraś cēti saptārthaḥ. cuṇaō viaraō iti dhanapālaḥ. āghrātārthē ’pīti kēcit || [ 22 ]

cañcuculuēsu cuñculi avagamiasaïṇṇhayāsu cuñculiaṁ |

cuñcuṇiā ciapaḍiravaramaṇambilimuṭṭhijūajūāsu || 23 ||

cuñculī cañcuśculukaś ca. cuñculi iti luptavibhaktyantō nirdēśaḥ. cuñculiaṁ ava dhāritaṁ satr̥ṣṇatā ca. cuñcuṇiā cyutaṁ pratiravō ramaṇamamlikā muṣṭidyūtaṁ yūkā cēti ṣaḍarthā. pratirava iti sāmānyaśabdō ’pi viśēṣē gōṣṭhīpratiravē vartatē. yadāha. || cuñcuṇiā pratiravō gōṣṭhayām || kēcit cuñcuṇiaṁ calitē ’pyāhuḥ || [ 23 ]

challī tajāi chaddī sējjāē vijjulāi chaḍā |

kavikacchū chaṅkuichuñchuīu chaliā chaïllachappaṇṇā || 24 ||

challī tvak. chaddī śayyā. chaḍā vidyut. atra chaṇō utsava iti kṣaṇaśa bdabhavō 'yam itinōktaḥ. chaṅkuī tathā chuñchuī kapikacchuḥ. chaliō chaïllō chappasō ity ētē trayō ’pi vidagdhārthāḥ. anyōnyaparyāyabhaṅgayā tu nibaddhāḥ. yathā–

kayalīchalliṁ chaṅkuimambujachaddiṁ pi chuñchuiṁ muṇaï |

chaliēṇa chaïllapiā tēṇa viṇā chaḍacalēṇa chappaṇṇā || 20 || [ 24 ]

chavaḍī cammaṁ chappantī ṇiamō jattha lihiaē paümaṁ |

taṇuē chaüacchikkōliā chamalaō a sattachaē || 25 ||

chavaḍī carma. chappantī niyamaviśēṣō yatra padmaṁ likhyatē. chaüaṁ tathā chikkō liaṁ tanu. chamalaō saptacchadaḥ. yathā–

jassa kaē chappantiṁ karōsi chaüaṅgi sō vi tujjha kaē |

chamalayatalammi chikkōliūṇa millēi migachavaḍiṁ || 29 ||

atra. chaḍḍaï muñcati. chajjaï rājati. iti dhātvādēśēṣūktāviti nōktau.

khandē chaḍakkharō vi hu chāsī takkammi ricchaē chārō |

chāhī khē chāīō māīō lahuamacchaē chiddō || 26 ||

chaḍakkharō skandaḥ. chāsī takram. chārō acchabhallaḥ. chāhī gaganam. chāyāvācakas tu chāhīśabdaśrchāyāśabda-bhava ēva. chāīō mātaraḥ. chiddō laghu matsyaḥ. yathā–

chāichaḍakkharachāhīmaṇi ṇa paṇamēsi kahasu kassa kaē |

chāsīhāriṇi dhūē chārasirē chiddagandhillē || 22 || [ 26 ]

chillī sihāi chittaṁ chiviē jārēsu chiṇṇachiṇṇālā |

chivvaṁ kārimamucchudalē chiviaṁ vāhalīi chiñchōlī || 27 ||

chillī śikha. chittaṁ spr̥ṣṭam. chiṇṇō tathā chiṇṇālō jāraḥ. jārēṣvityēkaśēṣā dbahuvacanāt chiṇṇā chiṇṇālī strītyapi. chivvaṁ kr̥trimam. chiviaṁ ikṣukhaṇḍam. chiñchōlī vāhalī. vāhalīśabdaś ca laghujalapravāhavācakō dēśya ēva vakṣyatē. yathā–

chivvasiṇēhacchittacchilliṁ chiviēṇa bhōliūṇa sisuṁ |

jaṁ calasi ghaḍakarā taṁ chiṇṇē chiñchōliāi chiṇṇālō || 23 || [ 27 ]

chippīraṁ ca palālē chippālō sassasattaüsahammi |

chillaramavi pallalaē muhavikkōṇē a chivvōllō || 28 ||

chippīraṁ palālam. chippālō sasyāsaktō gauḥ. chillaraṁ palvalam. chivvō llō nindārthaṁ mukhavikūṇanam. vikūṇitaṁ mukhamēvētyanyē. yathā–

tujjha kaē bāhēhiṁ sā chillarayaṁ bharēi duṭṭha tumaṁ |

chivvōllēṇa tamikkhasi chippīratiṇaṁ va chippālō || 24 ||

atra. chivaï chihaï spr̥śati. ētau dhātvādēśēṣūktāviti nōktau. [ 28 ]

chippāluachikkōaṇachihaṇḍayā pucchaasahaṇadahisarā |

chiṇṇōbbhavā ya duvvā taha chiṇṇacchōḍaṇaṁ sigghē || 29 ||

chippāluaṁ puccham. chikkōaṇō asahanaḥ. chihaṇḍaō dadhisaraḥ. chiṇṇōbbhavā dūrvā. chiṇṇacchōḍaṇaṁ śīghram. yathā–

varachippālua chiṇṇōbbhavāchihaṇḍēhi dhavala puṭṭhō si |

chiṇṇacchōḍaṇagamaṇē hakkāchikkōaṇō havasu iṇhiṁ || 25 || [ 29 ]

dahiē chihiṇḍibhillaṁ chiñchaṭaramaṇaṁ ca miñcaṇakkīlā |

chundaṁ bahuammi balāyāi chuī littaē chuhiaṁ || 30 ||

chihiṇḍibhillaṁ dadhi. chiñchaṭaramaṇaṁ cakṣuḥsthaganakrīḍā. chudaṁ bahu. chuī balā kā. chuhiaṁ liptam. yathā–

chundaghaṇacchuhiaṁ ṇahamuḍḍīṇāchihiṇḍibhilladhavalachuiṁ |

jāva huaṁ tā tīē chiñchaṭaramaṇaṁ sahīhi kayaṁ || 29 || [ 30 ]

churiachuramaḍḍichuñchummusayā maṭṭichurahatthaaraīsu |

chēṇḍī lahuracchāē chēlī thōvappasūṇamālāē || 31 ||

churiā mr̥ttiā. churamaḍḍī kṣurahastaḥ. nāpita iti yāvat. churahatthaśabdō ’pi dēśyaḥ. paryāyabhaṅgayā tūpāttaḥ. chuñchummusayaṁ raṇaraṇakaḥ. chēṇḍī laghurathyā. chēlī alpaprasūnā mālā. yathā–

juttaṁ chuñchummusayaṁ karēsi churamaḍḍiāi churahattha |

chēli ccia aṇurūvā churiāghaḍiassa chēṇḍijakkhassa || 27 || [ 31 ]

chēttaramaṇavvasuppāi chēbhaō hatthabimbammi |

chāgammi chēlaō khēttajāgarē chēttasōvaṇayaṁ || 32 ||

chēttaraṁ jīrṇaṁ śrūrpādyupakaraṇam. chēbhaō sthāsakaḥ. chēlaō chāgaḥ. kapratya yābhāvē chēlōity api. chēttasōvaṇayaṁ kṣētrē jāgaraṇam. yathā–

masichēbhaïllavasaṇaṁ parihariuṁ chēttaraṁ va maṁ bahiṇi |

tīi kaē sō chēlō ṇisi vaccaï chēttasōvaṇamisēṇa || 28 || [ 32 ]

chōbbhō pisuṇō dāsammi chōiō appiammi chōbbhatthaṁ |

chaṇṭō jalacchaḍāsigghēsuṁ chāō a bhukkhiakisēsu || 33 ||

chōbbhō piśrunaḥ. kēcit chōbbhō khala iti pūrvadēśīṣu pāṭhaṁ dr̥ṣṭvā khalaśabdavi pralabdhāḥ khalaṁ piṇyākaṁ vyācakṣata udāharanti ca. asmābhis tu sārataradēśīparyā lōtanēna chōbbhō piśruna iti dr̥ṣṭamudāhr̥taṁ ca. tatra bahudr̥śvānaḥ pramāṇam. chōiō dāsaḥ. chōbbhatthaṁ apriyam. hrasvaḥ saṁyōgē. iti chubbhatthaṁ ity api. yathā.

tīē kaḍillavatthaṁ uttariaṁ karia majjha daṁsantō |

kiṁ kāhisi iha asaṁ rē chōia chōbbha chōbbhatthaṁ || 29 ||

chaṇṭō jalacchaṭā śīghraś cēti vdyarthaḥ. chāō bubhukṣitaḥ kr̥śaś ca. nanu. chātōdarī yuvadr̥śāṁ kṣaṇamutsavō ’bhūt ||ity ādau chātaśabdasya kr̥śārthasya darśanātkathamayaṁ dēśyaḥ. naivam. chēdanārthasyaiva chātaśabdasya sādhutvāt. na ca dhātvanēkārthatā. uttaramatra. anēkārthatā hi dhātūnāṁ lōkaprasidhdyā. lōkē ca chātaśabdasya chēdanārthaṁ muttkāsyaiva kavēḥ prayōgō nānyēṣāmityalaṁ bahunā || [ 33 ]

dhaṇṇāīṇaṁ malaṇē gōmayavatthēsu taha chāṇaṁ |

chāyā kittībhamarīsu chārayaṁ ucchusakkamaülēsu || 34 ||

chāṇaṁ dhānyādimalanaṁ gōmayaṁ vastraṁ cēti tryartham. chāṇītyapi kēṣāñcitpāṭhaḥ. chāyā kīrttirbhramarī ca. chārayaṁ ikṣuśalkaṁ mukulaṁ ca || [ 34 ]

chāillō a paīvē sarisē ūṇē surūvē a |

chiddakuḍīsuṁ chillaṁ chiṇḍaṁ sihachattadhūvajantēsu || 35 ||

chāillō pradīpaḥ sadr̥śa ūnaḥ surūpaś cēti caturarthaḥ. chillaṁ chidraṁ kuṭī ca. chillaṁ vr̥tyantaramapīti kēcit. chiṇḍaṁ cūḍā chatraṁ dhūpayantraṁ ca. saṁyōgē para idētōḥ kāmacāra iti chēḍaṁ ity api || [ 35]

chippaṁ bhikkhāpucchēsu chittachīēsu chikkaṁ ca |

chivaō samūhaṇīvīsu chiñchaō dēhajārēsu || 36||

chippaṁ bhikṣā pucchaṁ va. chikkaṁ spr̥ṣṭaṁ kṣutaṁ ca. chivaō samūhō nīvī ca. chiñchaō dēhō jāraś ca. kēcit chiñchayaṁ śalāṭuphalamāhuḥ. yathā–

dhūāi paḍhamagabbhaṁ va rakkhaē uaha āḍhiā ghariṇī |

tumbīi paḍhamaṇiggayamābandhurabandhaṇaṁ chiñchaṁ || 30 || [ 36 ]

chippantī vayaūsavabhēē piṭṭhē vi chippiṇḍī |

chikkōṭṭalī a payaravapāmaddāchāṇakhaṇaḍēsu || 37 ||

chippantī vratabhēda utsava-bhēdaś cēti dvyarthā. chippiṇḍī vratōtsavabhēdau piṣṭaṁ cēti vyarthā. chikkōṭṭalī aṁhriravaḥ pādābhyāṁ dhānyamalanaṁ gōmayakhaṇḍaṁ cēti tryarthā || [ 37 ]

chippandūraṁ gōmayakhaṇḍammi tahēa visamammi |

sisusasisu chuddahīrō chēō antammi diarē a || 38 ||

chippandūraṁ gōmayakhaṇḍaṁ viṣamaṁ cēti dvyartham. chuddahīrō śiśruḥ śaśī ca. chēō antō dēvaraś ca || [ 38 ]

chēdhō thāsayacōrēsu sihāṇōmāliāsu chēṇḍā vi |

chōhō gaṇavikkhēvā chōbbhāittī achēppabēsāsu || 39 ||

chēdhō sthāsakaścauraś ca. chēṇḍā śikhā navamālikā ca. chōhō samūhō vikṣēpaï chōbbhāittī aspr̥śyā dvēṣyā va || [ 39 ]

jaṅgā gōarabhūmī jaccō purisē tusē jambhō |

jayaṇaṁ hayakavacammi jaraṇḍō vuḍḍhammi jaṇahalī ṇīvī || 40

jaṅgā gōcarabhūmiḥ. jaccō puruṣaḥ. jambhō tuṣaḥ. jayaṇaṁ hayasannāhaḥ. jaraṁ br̥ddhaḥ. jaraḍōity anyē. jaṇhalī nīvī. yathā–

jayaṇēhi hayā gāmā jaṅgāhi kaṇā a jambhabhāvēṇa |

mahilāō jaṇhalīhi sahanti gēhā jaraṇḍajaccēhiṁ || 31 || [ 40 ]

jaḍiaṁ khaciē jagalaṁ paṅkasurē jambulō a vāṇīrē |

ṇāṅgalasihāi javaṇaṁ jaḍammi jambhalajahājāyā || 41 ||

jaḍiaṁ khacitam. jagalaṁ paṅkilā surā. paṅkilasarakō jagalaṁ ity anyē. jambulō vānīraḥ. jambulaṁ madyabhājanam itisātavāhanaḥ. javaṇaṁ halaśikhā. jambhalō tathā jahājāō jaḍaḥ. yathā–

maṇijaḍiavāsabhavaṇē jagalaṁ jambulagharōciaṁ ṇintō |

jahajāya kīsa lajjasi javaṇōciahatthajambhalattēṇa || 32 ||

atra jagarō sannāha iti saṁskr̥tasamaḥ. jampaï kathayati. javaï yāpayati. iti dhātvādēśēṣūktāviti nōktau. [ 41 ]

jahimā viaḍḍhagāhā javayajavarayā javaṅkuraē |

jaṅghāmaō a jaṅghāluammi jambālayaṁ ca jalaṇīlī || 42 ||

jahimā vidagdharacitā gāthā. javaō tathā javaraō yavāṅkuraḥ. jaṅghāmaō tathā jaṅghāluō dvāvapyētāvanyōnyaparyāyatayā jaṅghālavācakau. jambālaṁ jalanīlī. śēvālamityarthaḥ. jalanīlīśabdō yadi saṁskr̥tē na rūḍhastadā dēśyaḥ. yathā–

jaṅghāluē ṇaïaḍaṁ gayā si jaṁ tuha taṇummi jambālō |

taha javarayagōvīō tuha jahimaṁ tattha gāyanti || 33||

taṁ javayagōraaṅgiṁ bhariuṁ jaṅghāmaō havia vacca |

jalaṇīliduggamaggō ṇa viambhaï pāusō jāva || 34 || [ 42 ]

jacchandaō satantammi jakkharattī a dīvālī |

jaṇṇōhaṇō ṇisiarē jaṅghāchēō a caccaraē || 43||

jacchandaō svacchandaḥ. kapratyayābhāvē jacchandō. jakkharattī dīpālikā. jaṇṇōhaṇō rākṣasaḥ. jaṅghāchēō catvaram. yathā–

maṇivalaēhi kuṇantī jaṅghāchēammi jakkharattiṁ va |

jaṇṇōhaṇāṇa vi tumaṁ ṇisi jacchandēṇa kiṁ ḍarasi || 35 || [ 43 ]

viddaviammi jagaḍiō jambhaṇaāī jahicchabhaṇirāī |

jaraladdhiajaralaviā gāmīṇē ūruē jahaṇarōhō || 44 ||

jagaḍiō vidrāvitaḥ. kadarthita ity arthaḥ. jambhaṇaō yathēṣṭavaktā. jambhaṇabhaṇō iti kēcit. ubhayatrādigrahaṇāt. jampicchaō yathādr̥ṣṭamabhilaṣita. jampōcchiramaggirō yō yadyadr̥ṣṭaṁ tadēva mr̥gayatē. ityādi. atra. jaaḍaï tvaratē. iti dhātvādēśēṣūkta m itinōktam. jaraladdhiō tathā jaralaviō grāmīṇaḥ. jahaṇarōhō ūruḥ. yathā–

jaraladdhiāi daṭṭhuṁ pavaṇalhasantaṁsuaṁ jahaṇaṇēhaṁ |

ō kāmasarajagaḍiā jaralaviā hunti jambhaṇayā || 36 || [ 44 ]

jahaṇūsavamaddhōrū jaṅkayasukaō 'ppasukayagijjhammi |

jāḍī gummaṁ jāī surā kaviṭṭhammi jāūrō || 45||

jahaṇūsavaṁ ardhōrukam. jaṅkayasukaō alpasukr̥tagrāhyaḥ. jāḍī gulmam. jāī surā. jāūrō kapitthaḥ. yathā–

jāūrajāḍikaṇṭayaphaṭṭirajahaṇūsavā vi tēṇa samaṁ |

jāīluddhā vaccasi jaṅkayasukayā si taṁ putti || 37 || [ 45 ]

jālaghaḍiā siraharē jigghiamōsiṅghiatthammi |

jiṇṇōbbhavā ya duvvāi jīvayamaī a vāhamaī || 46 ||

jālaghaḍiā candraśālā. jigghiaṁ ghrātam. atra jimiaṁ bhuktam itibhujidhā tvādēśabhavam. jiṇṇōbbhavā dūrvā. jīvayamaī mr̥gākarṣaṇahēturvyādhamr̥gī. yathā–

jālaghaḍiāi jā taṁ ṇa ṇiasi jīvayamaïṁ va mayaṇassa |

tā bhama hariṇō vva tumaṁ kulaḍājiṇṇōbbhavāu jigghantō || 38 || [ 46 ]

atra jīhaï lajjatē. iti dhātvādēśēṣūktam itinōktam.

juṇṇō chēgē jualō taruṇē apariggahammi juñjuruḍō |

jualiajurumillā duguṇiagahaṇā juaō a bappīhē || 47 ||

juṇṇō vidagdhaḥ. jualō taruṇaḥ. juñjuruḍō aparigrahaḥ. jualiaṁ dviguṇitam. jurumillaṁ gahanam. jūrummilayaṁ iti gōpālaḥ . juaō cātakaḥ. yathā–

juñjuruḍāē ghaṇaravajualiavisamasaravēaṇāi maha |

duhajurumillāvatthaṁ kaha jūaa tassa juṇṇajualassa || 39 ||

atra. jūravaï vañcati. iti dhātvādēśēṣūktam itinōktam || [ 47 ]

jēmaṇayaṁ dāhiṇaē aṅgē jō raṁ ca jō kiratthammi |

jōkkhamacōkkhē jōō candē jōggā ya cāḍummi || 48 ||

jēmaṇayaṁ dakṣiṇamaṅgam. hastādi. jō raṁ yaḥ kirētyarthē. jōkkhaṁ malinam. jōō candraḥ. jōggā cāṭu. yathā–

jayasiriṇivāsajēmaṇabhua tuha guṇavasaṇammi kā jōggā |

jō raṁ jasēṇa cālukka jōkkhamavaharasi jōassa || 40 || [ 48 ]

ṇakkhattē jōḍaṁ jōisaṁ ca jōī a vijjūē |

khaliammi jōirō jōikkhō dīvammi jōḍiō vāhē || 49||

jōḍaṁ tathā jōisaṁ nakṣatram. jōī vidyut. jōirō skhalitaḥ. jōikkhō dīpaḥ. jōḍiō vyādhaḥ. yathā–

mēhammi pihiajōisavaïjōḍē ruirajōijōikkhē |

hiṇḍanti ajōirayā vammahajōḍiasarāhayā kulaḍā || 41 || [ 49 ]

ṇayaṇammi jōaṇaṁ taha khajjōē jōiaṁ jāṇa |

jōiṅgaṇō a indōvē jōvārīi jōsaliā || 50||

jōaṇaṁ lōcanam. jōiō khadyōtaḥ. jōiṅgaṇō indragōpaḥ. jōṇṇaliā jōvārī. dhānyam. jōvārīśabdō ' pi dēśya ēva. yathā–

calajōiajōiṅgaṇamikkhia jōṇṇaliakāraṇaṁ kālaṁ |

kāsayavahūu harisā upphullayajōaṇā hunti || 42 || [ 50 ]

jōvvaṇaṇīraṁ taha jōvvaṇavēaṁ jōvvaṇōvayaṁ ca jarā |

jaṇhaṁ lahupiḍharē kasiṇaē a jampaṇamakittivayaṇēsu || 51||

jōvvaṇaṇīraṁ tathā jōvvaṇavēṇaṁ tathā jōvvaṇōvayaṁ vayaḥ pariṇāmaḥ. jōvvaṇa ṇīrō jōvvaṇōvaō r̥r̥kṣa iti catuṣpadavargē yatkēnaciduktaṁ tasya sammōha ēva. yathā–

jōvvaṇaṇīraṁ taruṇakṣaṇē vi vijiēndiāṇa purisāṇa |

jōvvaṇavēē vi ṇa jōvvaṇōvayaṁ hōi iarāṇa || 43 ||

jaṇhaṁ laghupiṭharaṁ kr̥ṣṇaṁ cēti dvyartham. jampaṇaṁ akīrtirvaktraṁ ca || [ 51 ]

vēḍisavaruṇēsuṁ jambuō a gāmaṇiviḍēsu jaṇaüttō |

jaccandaṇamagarū kuṅkumaṁ ca jōvō a binduthōvēsu || 52 ||

jambuō vētasavr̥kṣaḥ paścimadikpālaś ca. jaṇaüttō grāmapradhānapuruṣō viṭaś ca. jaccandaṇaṁ agaruḥ kuṅkumaṁ ca. jōvō binduḥ stōkaṁ ca. atra jūraï khidyatē krudhyati cēti dhātvādēśēṣūktam itinōktam || [ 52 ]

santatavarisammi jhaḍī jhaṅkhō tuṭṭhē jhalā ya mayataṇhā |

jhaṇṭī lahuddhakēsēsu pīlumāyāsu jhaṇḍuajhamālā || 53 ||

jhaḍī nirantaravr̥ṣṭiḥ. jhaṅkhō tuṣṭaḥ. jhalā mr̥gatr̥ṣṇā. jhaṇṭī laghūrdhvakēśāḥ. jhaṇḍuō pīluvr̥kṣaḥ. jhamālaṁ indrajālam. yathā–

ṇa jhaḍiṁ jhaṅkhō vi ravī kuṇaï jhalaṁ cēa ittha marudēsē |

muñca jhamālāi lulantajhaṇṭiō jhaṇḍuāi cuṇṭēsu || 44 || [ 53 ]

jhaṇḍalijhaṅkharajharayā asaīsukkatarusuṇṇaārēsu |

jhajjharijharuā khikkhirimasaēsuṁ jhampaṇī pamhē || 54||

jhaṇḍalī asatī. jhaṅkharō śuṣkataruḥ. jharaō suvarṇakāraḥ. jhajjharī sparśapa rihārārthaṁ caṇḍālādīnāṁ hastayaṣṭiḥ. khikkhirīti. jharuō maśakaḥ. maśakavācaka śabdāścīryāmapi vartantē. yad āha— maśakākhyāścīryāmapyucyantē kāvyatattvajñaiḥ. iti. jhaṁraṇī pakṣma. yathā–

jharuāulammi mīliajhampaṇiaṁ jhajjharīkaravirūvaṁ |

jhaṅkharatalammi jharayāhamaṁ hahā jhaṇḍalī ramaï || 45 || [ 54 ]

vayaṇijjē jhakkiajhiṅkhiā jharaṅkō a tiṇapurisē |

jhaṇṭiajhaṇṭaliāō pahariacaṅkamaṇaatthēsu || 55 ||

jhakkiaṁ tathā jhiṅkhiaṁ vacanīyam. ujjhiṅkhiaṁ vacanīyam ititu utpūrvēṇa jhiṅkhiaśabdēna siddham. jharaṅkō tr̥ṇamayaḥ puruṣaḥ. jharantō iti kēcit. jhaṇṭiaṁ prahr̥tam. jhaṇṭaliā caṅkamaṇam. yathā–

ṇa kuṇanti jhaṇṭiaṁ ṇa ya jhaṇṭaliaṁ jhakkiāi agaṇantā |

tuha kumaravāla riuṇō ajhiṅkhia raṇājirē jharaṅka vva || 46 ||

atra. jhaḍaï śīyatē. jhampaï bhramatītyādayō dhātvādēśēṣūktā iti nōktāḥ. [ 55 ]

daḍḍhammi jhalusiaṁ taha jhaluṅkiaṁ jhāmiaṁ cēa |

jhaṅkāriajhaṅkhariā avacayaṇē jhōliāi jhalajhaliā || 56 ||

jhalusiaṁ jhaluṅkiaṁ jhāmiaṁ trayamapi dagdhārtham. jhaṅkāriaṁ tathā jhaṅkhariaṁ avacayanam. jhalajhaliā jhōlikā. jhōlikāśabdō yadi saṁskr̥tē na rūjhastadāyamapi dēśyaḥ. yathā–

tāvajhaluṅkiadavajhalusiō tuha payāvajhāmiō a riū |

phalajhaṅkāriadalajhaṅkhariāiṁ kuṇaï jhalajhaliahatthō || 47 || [ 56 ]

jhāḍaṁ layagahaṇē jhāmarō jarī jhāulaṁ ca vaüṇiphalē |

jhāruajhiriṇḍajhīrā cīrījarakūvalajjāsu || 57 ||

jhāḍaṁ latāgahanam. jhāmarō pravayāḥ. jhāulaṁ karpāsaphalam. jhāruā cīrī. jhiriṇḍaṁ jīrṇakūpaḥ. jhīrā lajjā. yathā–

jhāulacuṇṭaṇakajjē ajhīra kaha jhāmaraṁ ṇiōēsi |

jhāruajjhāḍacchasē jhiriṇḍaē ēsa jaṁ paḍihī || 48 || [ 57 ]

jhuṅkhō vajjavisēsē jhuttī chēammi jhuṭṭhamaliammi |

jhullurijhuṇṭaṇajhuñjhummusayā gummappavahamaṇaduhēsu || 58||

jhuṅkhō tuṇayākhyō vādyaviśēṣaḥ. jhuttī chēdaḥ. jhuṭṭhaṁ alīkam. jhullurī gulmaḥ. jhuṇṭaṇaṁ pravāhaḥ. atra jhuṇaï jugupsatē. iti dhātvādēśēṣuktam itinōktam. jhuñjhummusayaṁ manōduḥkham. jhumujhumusayaṁ ity anyē. yathā–

tuha ṇatthi jhuṭṭhajhuttī jhuṇṭaṇataḍajhullurīsu ṇāō si |

jhuñjhummusayavaīē maha kahiaṁ tattha jhuṅkhavāēhiṁ || 49 || [ 58 ]

jhūraṁ kuḍilē jhērō jagaghaṇṭē jhēṇḍuō vi kaṇḍuaē |

addhamahisīi jhōṭṭī jhōḍappō caṇayadhalaṇṇammi || 59 ||

jhūraṁ kuṭilam. atra jhūraï smaratīti dhātvādēśēṣūktam itinōktam. jhērō jaraghaṇṭaḥ. jhēṇḍuō kandukaḥ. jhōṭṭī ardhamahiṣī. jhōḍappō caṇakadhānyam. śruṣka caṇakaśākamityanyē. yathā–

jhōḍappachēttakaṇṭhē jhōṭṭīō kaṇṭhabaddhajhērāō |

ua cāraï gōvavahū khēllantī jhēṇḍuēṇa jhūragaī || 50 || [ 59 ]

vāhammi jhōḍiō jhōṇḍaliā rāsayasaricchakīlāē |

ṭaṅkacchiṇṇājasataḍataḍatthadīhagahirēsu jhasasaddō || 60 ||

jhōḍiō vyādhaḥ. jhōṇḍaliā rāsakasadr̥śī krīḍā. yathā–

jhōṇḍaliāē khēllantu tāva bālāu hariṇiāu vva |

ārōviūṇa cāvaṁ paharēi ṇa kāmajhōḍiō jāva || 59 ||

jhasō ṭaṅkacchinnamayaśastaṭastaṭasthō dīrghagambhīraś cēti pañcārthaḥ || [ 60 ]

gayaṇaṭṭhēsuṁ jharthaṁ ca jhampiaṁ tuṭṭhaghaṭṭiēsuṁ ca |

jhasuraṁ tambōlatthēsū jhaṇḍulī asaïkīlāsu || 61 ||

jhatthaṁ gataṁ naṣṭaṁ ca. jhampiaṁ truṭitaṁ ghaṭṭitaṁ ca. jhasuraṁ tāmbūlamarthaś ca. jhaṇḍulī asatī krīḍā ca || [ 61 ]

palhatthākuṭṭhēsuṁ jhasiaṁ cīhimasaēsu jhilliriā |

aṅgakiḍaēsu jhīṇaṁ accatthē acchaē a jhūsariaṁ || 62 ||

jhasiaṁ paryastamākruṣṭaṁ ca. atra jhaṅkhaï santapyatē vilapati upālabhatē niḥśvasiti ca. jharaï smarati kṣarati cēti dhātvādēśēṣūktam itinōktam. jhilliriā cīhī tr̥ṇaṁ maśakaś ca. jhīṇaṁ aṅgaṁ kīṭaś ca. jhūsariaṁ atyarthaṁ svacchaṁ ca || [ 62 ]

ṭamarō kēsacaē caṅkiaṁ pasariē vimōḍaṇē ṭasaraṁ |

ṭasarōṭṭaṁ sēharaē ṭaṭṭaïā javaṇiāē a || 1 ||

ṭamarō kēśacayaḥ. ṭaṅkiaṁ prasr̥tam. ṭasaraṁ vimōṭanam. ṭasarōṭṭaṁ śēkharaḥ. ṭaṭṭaïā tiraskariṇī. yathā–

mā saṇṭhavēsu ṭamarē ṭasariacūaṅkurāṇa ṭasōraṭṭaṁ |

ṭaṅkiamayaṅkajuṇhāi antarē dēsu māmi ṭaṭṭaïaṁ || 1 || [ 1 ]

ṭambaraō bhāriaē karālakaṇṇammi ṭapparaō |

araṇiakusumē ṭakkāriā ya ṭārō ahamaturaē || 2 ||

ṭambaraō bhārikaḥ. gururityarthaḥ. ṭapparaō karālakarṇaḥ. ṭakkārī araṇiku sumam. ṭārō adhamaturaṅgaḥ. yathā–

ṭārammi caḍiamittō ṭambaraō ṭapparō a vāmaṇaō |

jhatti paḍiō hasijjaï ṭakkarīcuṇṭaṇīhi vaṇē || 2 || [ 2 ]

ṭippī ṭikkaṁ tilaē ṭimbaru tumburu ca ṭiggharō thērē |

ṭuṇṭō chiṇṇakarē ṭēṇṭā jūapayammi ṭēkkaraṁ ca thalē || 3 ||

ṭippī tathā ṭikkaṁ tilakam. ṭikkaṁ śirasi stabaka ity anyē. ṭimbaru tumburu | ṭiggharō sthaviraḥ. atra. ṭiviḍikkaï maṇḍayati. ṭiriṭillaï bhrāmyati. ētau dhātvā dēśēṣūktāviti nōktau. ṭuṇṭō chitrakaraḥ. ṭēṇṭā dyūtasthānam. ṭēkkaraṁ sthalam. yathā–

candaṇaṭikkiaparavahumiha ṭēkkarēē ramantiaṁ dadda‌uṁ |

ṭimbarujōggaya ṭiggharaṭuṇṭayaṭēṇṭia karēsi kiṁ ṭippiṁ || 3 || [ 3 ]

ṭōlō salahē ṭōlambaṭōkkaṇā mahuamajjabhaṇḍēsu |

asichisakhāyajaṅghākhaṇittabhittītaḍēsu ṭaṅkō vi || 4 ||

ṭōlō śalabhaḥ. ṭōlō piśāca ity anyē. yad āha— ṭōlaṁ piśācam āhuḥ sarvē śalabhaṁ tu rāhulakaḥ || ṭōlambō madhūkaḥ. ṭōkkaṇaṁ madyaparimāṇabhāmḍam. kēcit cōkkaṇakhaṇḍaṁ madyamānabhāṇḍamāhuḥ. yathā–

ṭōlō vva mā paḍa tumaṁ ujjāṇē vāṇiṇīu jaṁ puraō |

ṭōlambavaṇē ṭōkkaṇahatthā mayaṇaggijālāō || 4 ||

ṭakō khaṅgaśrchinnaṁ khātaṁ jaṅghā khanitraṁ bhittistaṭaṁ cēti saptārthaḥ || [ 4 ]

ṭhallayaṭhaïaṭṭhaviā ṇiddhaṇaükkhittapaḍimāsu |

ṭhāṇō māṇē ṭhāṇijjō gōraviammi siṇhaē ṭhikkaṁ || 5 ||

ṭhallō nirdhanaḥ. ṭhaïō utkṣiptaḥ. ṭhaïō avakāśa ity anyē. ṭhaviā pratimā. ṭhāṇō mānaḥ. ṭhāṇijjō gauravitaḥ. ayaṁ dantyādirapītyēkē. thāṇijjō. ṭhikkaṁ śiśnam. yathā–

ṭhāṇē ṇa ṭhallayāṇaṁ ṭhāṇijjattaṁ ṇa yāvi ṭhaïāṇaṁ |

ṇa ya ṭhikkaṁ saṇḍhāṇaṁ aṭhaviaüvalāṇa ṇa ya pūā || 5 || [ 5 ]

gōraviuddhēsuṁ ṭhariaṁ ṭhiviaṁ uddhaṇiaḍahikkāsu |

dantaggahiē ḍakkaṁ ḍavvō ḍāvō a vāmakarē || 6 ||

ṭhariaṁ gauravitamūrdhvasthitaṁ ca. ṭhiviaṁ ūrdhvaṁ nikaṭaṁ hikkā cēti tryartham ūrdhvārthē ṭhiaaṁ ity anyē.

ḍakkaṁ dantagr̥hītam. daṣṭārthaṁ tu daṣṭaśabda-bhavam. ḍavbō tathā ḍāvō vāmakaraḥ. yathā–

ḍavvē pharayamaḍāvē khaggaṁ gahiūṇa tuha paī samarē |

pahupaccakkhaṁ pasaraï amarisaḍakkāharō ēsō || 6 || [ 6 ]

ḍaṇḍaṁ ḍiṇḍī sīviakappaḍakhaṇḍēsu taha ḍalō lōṭṭhē |

ḍapphaṁ sēllē ḍallaṁ piḍiāi aliñjarē ḍaharī || 7 ||

ḍaṇḍaṁ tathā ḍiṇḍī sūcyā saṅghaṭitāni vastrakhaṇḍāni. ḍaṇḍītyapyanyē. ḍalō lōṣṭaḥ. ḍapphaṁ sēllākhyamāyudham. ḍallaṁ piṭikā. ḍaharī aliñjaram. yathā–

ḍaṇḍaparihāṇaḍiṇḍīpāuraṇā caïa ḍapphayā tujjha |

riuṇō pallivaṇiharē ḍaharīḍallē vahanti ḍalakhalirā || 7 || [ 7 ]

ḍaharō sisū siraharammi ḍaggalō davapahammi ḍaḍḍhāḍī |

racchāi ḍaṇḍaō ḍambhiō a kitavammi ḍambarō ghammē || 8||

ḍaharō śiśruḥ. ḍaggalō bhavanōpari bhūmitalam. ḍaḍḍhāḍī davamārgaḥ. ḍaṇḍaō rathyā. ḍambhiō dyūtakāraḥ. ḍambarō dharmaḥ. yathā–

giṇhia ḍaharē uttaria ḍaggalā ḍaṇḍaēṇa tuha riuṇō |

ḍaḍḍhāḍiḍambarillē janti vaṇē ḍambhia vva jaravasaṇā || 8 ||

atra. ḍallaï pibati. ḍaraï trasyati. ētau dhātvādēśēṣūktāviti nōktau || [ 8 ]

ḍālī sāhāē ṇāyaṇē ḍāalaḍōlaḍōaṇayā |

ḍialī thūṇā bhēgammi ḍiḍḍarō ḍimphiaṁ ca jalapaḍiē || 9 ||

ḍālī śākhā. ḍāalaṁ ḍōlō ḍōaṇaṁ trayō ’pi lōcanārthāḥ. ḍialī sthūṇā. ḍiḍḍarō bhēkaḥ. ḍimphiaṁ jalapatitam. yathā–

gayaḍōla ḍōaṇēhiṁ ṇa ṇiasi ḍāliṁ luṇēsi ḍialikaē |

tā taraliaḍāalaō guttidrahē ḍiḍḍarō vva ḍimphēsu || 9 ||

atra. ḍimbhaï sraṁsatē. iti dhātvādēśēṣūktam itinōktam || [ 9 ]

ḍiṇḍilliaṁ ca khaliē vatthē ḍīraṁ ca kandalaē |

ōiṇṇammi a ḍīṇaṁ tahēa ḍīṇōvayaṁ uvari || 10||

ḍiṇḍilliaṁ khalikhacitaṁ vastram. ḍiṇḍilliaṁ skhalitē hastē iti kēcit. yad āha— ḍimphiaḍiṇḍilliayā patitē ca skhalitahastē ca. ḍīraṁ kandalaḥ. ḍīṇaṁ avatīrṇam. uḍḍīnavācakas tu saṁskr̥tabhava ēva. ḍīṇōvayaṁ upari. yathā–

viṇhū ḍīṇō si tumaṁ baliṇivaḍīṇōvayaṁ payaṁ dēsi |

ḍīraṁ lihanti ḍiṇḍilliaṁ ca parihanti tēṇa tuha riuṇō || 10 || [ 10 ]

ḍumbō savacē ḍuṅghō uañcaṇē ḍuṅgarō sēlē |

ghaṇṭammi ḍuṇḍuō ḍōlā siviā dāruhatthaē ḍōō || 11||

ḍumbō śvapacaḥ. ḍuṅghō udañcanaviśēṣō nālikēranayaḥ. ḍuṅgarō śailaḥ. ḍuṇḍuō jīrṇaghaṇṭaḥ. ḍōlā śibikā. andōlanavācakakas tu dōlāśabda-bhavaḥ. ḍōō dāru hastaḥ. yathā–

ḍuṅgaraāṇiaḍōlāḍōē vikkintayassa tuha riuṇō |

ḍuṇḍuasarassa ḍumbō tti chivia ḍuṅghayajalēṇa lēi jaṇō || 11 || [ 11 ]

tambōlabhāyaṇē ḍōṅgilī tahā ḍōliō kasiṇāsārē |

ḍāū phalihaṁsadugē gaṇavaïpaḍimāvisēsē a || 12 ||

ḍōṅgilī tāmbūlabhājanaviśēṣaḥ. ḍōṅgilī tāmbūlinītyēkē. ḍiliō kr̥ṣṇa sāraḥ. yathā–

daïammi sāvarāhē ēntē ḍōliavisālaṇayaṇāē |

ḍōṅgiliṇihittavīḍayakaḍaḍḍhaṇamisaōḥ parammuhīi ṭhiaṁ || 12 ||

ḍāū phalihaṁsakavr̥kṣō gaṇapatipratimāviśēṣaś ca || [ 12 ]

ḍōṅgī a hatthabimbē tambōlaṭṭhāṇabhēē a |

ḍhaḍḍhō bhērī ḍhaṅkō a vāyasē ḍhaṇḍhaṇī a kavikacchū || 13 ||

ḍōṅgī sthāsakastāmbūlabhājanaviśēṣaś ca.

ḍhaḍḍhō bhērī. ḍhaṅkō vāyasaḥ. ḍhaṇḍhaṇī kapikacchūḥ. yathā–

gōsuṭṭhiaḍhaṅkaülē dēulavāijjamāṇaḍhaḍḍhē a |

uṭṭhaviō vēsāē ḍhaṇḍhaṇichittō vva tammaï bhuaṅgō || 13 || [ 13 ]

maṅkuṇaē ḍhaṅkuṇaḍhēṅkuṇā tahā ḍhaṅkaṇī pihāṇīē |

ḍhaṁsayamajasē vīṇāi ḍhaṅkharī ḍhakkayaṁ tilaē || 14 ||

ḍhaṅkuṇō tathā ḍhēṅkuṇō matkuṇaḥ. ḍhaṅkaṇī pidhānikā. ḍhaṁsayaṁ ayaśaḥ. ḍhaṅkharī vīṇābhēdaḥ. ḍhakkayaṁ tilakam. yathā–

ḍhaṅkharia ḍhaṅkuṇaharē imāi mā vacca ḍhakkayaṁ daṭṭhuṁ |

ḍhēṅkuṇakhaddhō ḍhaṅkaṇihaṇiō ṇīharasi ḍhaṁsayaṁ lahia || 14||

atra ḍhakkaï chādayati. ḍhaṁsaï vivartatē. iti dhātvādēśēṣūktāviti nōktau || [ 14 ]

cikkhallē ḍhaṇḍhariō ḍhaṇḍhasiō gāmajakkhammi |

ṇiccammi ḍhikkayaṁ ḍhiṇḍhayaṁ jalagaē balāiā ḍhēṅkī || 15 ||

ḍhaṇḍhariō kardamaḥ. ḍhaṇḍhasiō grāmayakṣaḥ. kēcit grāmavr̥kṣa ity ācakṣatē. yad āhuḥ — ḍhaṇḍhasiō ḍhaṇḍhariō grāmatarau kardamē cākhyē. atra. ḍhaṇḍhallaï bhramati. ḍhaṇḍhōlaï gavēṣayati. iti dhātvādēśēṣūktāviti nōktau. ḍhikkayaṁ nityam. ḍhiṇḍhayaṁ jalamadhyapatitam. ḍhēṅkī balākā. yathā–

ḍhaṇḍhasiapūaṇaparā ḍhēṅkīō bhaṇaï ḍhikkayaṁ kā vi |

ḍhiṭṭhō kaha vi maha paī ḍhiṇḍhō ḍhaṇḍhariakhuttō vā || 15 ||

atra. ḍhikkaï vr̥ṣabhō garjati. ḍhumaï ḍhusaï bhramati. iti dhātvādēśēṣūktā iti nōktāḥ || [ 15 ]

adhaṇē ḍhēllō ḍhēṇḍhiaḍhōṅgharayā dhūviabbhamiraēsu |

ḍhaṇḍhō paṅkaṇiratthē ḍhaṇḍharaḍhayarā pisāyaīsāsu || 16 ||

ḍhēllō nirdhanaḥ. ḍhēṇḍhiō dhūṣitaḥ. ḍhōṅgharō bhramaṇaśīlaḥ. yathā–

sirikumaravāla riuṇō tuha davaḍajjhantapīludhūmahayā |

ṇavaagaruḍhēṇḍhiāṇaṁ sumarantē ḍhēllaḍhōṅgharā raṇṇē || 16 ||

ḍhaṇḍhō paṅkō nirarthakaś cēti samāhāraḥ. ḍhaṇḍharō tathā ḍhayarō piśāca īrṣyāyāṁ cēti dvāvapi vdyarthau || [ 16 ]

piḍharōṇhajalēsuṁ ḍhamaraṁ ḍhēṅkā harisakūvayatulāsu |

ṇatthā ṇāsārajjū āuttē ṇavvaṇōvvā ya || 17 ||

ḍhamaraṁ piṭharamuṣṇajalaṁ cēti dvyartham. atra ḍhuṇḍhullaï bhramati gavēṣayati cēti dhā tvādēśēṣūkta iti nōktaḥ.

ḍhēṅkā harṣaḥ kūpatulā cēti vdyarthā.

ṇatthā nāsārajjuḥ. ṇavvō tathā ṇōvvō āyuktaḥ. yathā–

bhakkhantēṇaṁ gāmaṁ ṇatthārahiōsahēṇa va samaggaṁ |

ṇavva taē ṇōvvāṇaṁ asāṇa vi bhañjiō maggō || 17 || [ 17 ]

ṇaddhō ārūḍhē ṇandāṇandīṇandiṇīu gāīē |

parivañciammi ṇāḍiō a ṇaccira ramaṇasīlammi || 18 ||

ṇaddhō ārūḍhaḥ. ṇandā ṇandī ṇandiṇī trayō ’py ētē gōvācakāḥ. atra ṇakkhā nakhāḥ. ṇavi vaiparītyē. ṇaï avadhāraṇē. ētē śabdānuśāsanē sādhitā iti nōktāḥ. ṇaḍiō vañcitaḥ. khēdita ity anyē. ṇaccirō ramaṇaśīlaḥ. yathā–

ambaraṇaddhē mēhē ṇandāvālīṇa ṇandiṇīgōṭṭhē |

ṇa suṇēsi ṇaccirāṇaṁ jaï gīaṁ ṇandiputta ṇaḍiō si || 18 || [ 18 ]

maliṇammi ṇajjarō ṇandaṇō a bhiccammi ṇajjharō vimalē |

ṇalayamusīrē sīhē ṇandikkhō ṇandiaṁ ca sīharuē || 19 ||

ṇajjarō malinaḥ. ṇandaṇō bhr̥tyaḥ. ṇajjharō vimalaḥ. ṇalayaṁ uśīram. ṇandikkhō siṁhaḥ. ṇandiaṁ siṁharutam. yathā–

ṇajjharajasa tuha riuṇō ṇaravaïṇandikkha ṇandiaṁ sōuṁ |

ṇajjaravatthā ṇalayakarā māliaṇandaṇā havia janti || 19 || [ 19 ]

duhiammi ṇaddiō ṇaḍḍarī a bhēgammi mandirē ṇaliaṁ |

ṇaharī churīi ṇaḍulī kacchavaē ṇahamuhō ghuē || 20 ||

ṇaddiō duḥkhitaḥ. ṇaḍḍarī bhēkaḥ. ṇaliaṁ gr̥ham. ṇaharī kṣurikā. ṇaḍulī kacchapaḥ. dvitvē ṇaḍḍulīity api. ṇahamuhō ghūkaḥ. yathā–

ṇahamuhaṇaliē rasē rusaṁ sōūṇa tuha riuvahūṇaṁ |

ṇaharīhaya vva ṇaḍḍariṇaḍulīu vi ṇaddiā hunti || 20 ||

atra. ṇavara kēvalē. ṇavari ānantaryē. ētāvavyayau. ṇavvaï ṇajjaï jñā yatē. ṇaḍaï gupyati. ētē dhātvādēśēṣūktā iti nōktāḥ || [ 20 ]

jattha palāsalayāē jaṇēhi païṇāma pucchiā juvaī |

akahantī ṇihaṇijjaï ṇiamavisēsō ṇavat‍nayā sā || 21 ||

yad āha— niyamaviśēṣaś ca ṇavalayā jñēyā. ādāya palāśalatāṁ bhrāmyati lōkō ’khilō yasyām. pr̥ṣṭā patināma strī nihanyatē cāpyakathayantī. yathā–

dōlāvilāsasamaē pucchantīhiṁ sahīhi païṇāmaṁ |

laṭṭhīhi haṇijjantī vahuā ṇavalayavayaṁ bharaï || 21 || [ 21 ]

ṇavaria sahasā ōāiē ṇamasiaṁ taḍammi ṇahavallī |

ṇāvvāuttō bhōgī kaṇhē ṇakkhattaṇēmī a || 22 ||

ṇavaria sahasā. ṇamasiaṁ upayācitakam. ṇavasiaṁ ity anyē. ṇahavallī vidyut. ṇavvāuttō īśvaraḥ. niyōgituta ity anyē. ṇakkhattaṇēmī viṣṇuḥ. yathā–

ṇamasiasaēhi pāviasirīi ṇakkhattaṇōmisamamappaṁ |

ṇavaria ṇavvāuttaya mā muṇa ṇahavallicañcalā ēsā || 22 || [ 22 ]

jalabhavaphalabhēē ṇaïmāsayamucciṭṭhaē ṇavōddharaṇaṁ |

ṇāō gavviṭṭhē ṇāullō gōmī bilammi ṇārōṭṭō || 23 ||

ṇāimāsayaṁ jalōdbhavaḥ phalabhēdaḥ. ṇavōddharaṇaṁ ucchiṣṭam. ṇāō garviṣṭhaḥ. ṇāullō gōmān. ṇārōṭṭō bilam. kūsāra ity anyē. yathā–

ṇāulla ṇavōddharaṇēṇa tūsa mā visasu ṇāyaüḍḍaṇayaṁ |

dulahaṇaïmāsayakaē sayā vi gōhā ṇa hōi ṇārōṭṭhē || 23 || [ 23 ]

ṇālambī jūḍē ṇāhidāmamullōamajjhadāmammi |

ṇālampiamakkandē jahaṇammi a ṇāhivicchēō || 24||

ṇālambī kuntalaḥ. ṇāhidāmaṁ ullōcamadhyadāma. ṇālampiaṁ ākranditam. ṇāhivicchēō jaghanam. ṇāhīē vicchēō iti vākyamapi jaghanavācakam. yadāha || ṇāhīē vicchēō jaghanaṁ kaiścittu ṇāhivicchēō. yathā–

puṇajammē kusumāiṁ gayāi ṇālambiṇāhidāmēsu |

ia ṇālampantē tuha riūṇa pihuṇāhivicchēā || 24 || [ 24 ]

ṇāmōkkasiaṁ kajjē ṇijjaṇuvaṇṇā ya suttammi |

bhūē ṇiḍō haliddā ṇiggā ṇihasō a vammīē || 25 ||

ṇāmōkkasiaṁ kāryam. ṇijjō tathā ṇuvaṇṇō suptaḥ. ṇiḍō piśācaḥ. ṇiggā haridrā. ṇihasō valmīkaḥ. yathā–

ṇāmōkkasiaṁ tumaē kiṁ rē ṇiḍa ṇiggarāga ṇihasamuha |

tīē ccia jaṁ ṇāmaṁ lavasi ṇuvaṇṇō aṇijjō a || 25 || [ 25 ]

ṇihuṇaṁ vāvārē kāmiāi ṇihuā ya ṇijjharaṁ jusē |

ṇivahō sāmiddhīē ṇiaḍī ḍambhē ṇihūamavi suraē || 26 ||

ṇihuṇaṁ vyāpāraḥ. ṇihuā kābhitā. ṇijjharaṁ jīrṇam. ṇijjhūraṁ ity anyē. ṇivahō samr̥ddhiḥ. ṇiaḍī dambhaḥ. yadi nikr̥tiśabdasya pratyādau [ siddhahēma° 1, 206 ] pāṭha iṣyatē tadā na dēśyaḥ. ṇihūaṁ suratam. yathā–

ṇihuāṇihūayāṇaṁ mā sambhara muñca ṇiaḍiṇihuṇāiṁ |

jaṁ ṇijjharō si iṇhiṁ kuṇasu maṇaṁ puṇṇaṇivahammi || 26 || [ 26 ]

tuṇhikkammi ṇiukkō ṇirulī mayarākiiggāhē |

ṇihaṇaṁ kūlē ṇigaḍhō dhammē ṇisuaṁ ṇisāmiaṁ ca suē || 27 ||

ṇiukkō tūṣṇīkaḥ. ṇirulī makarākr̥tigrāhaḥ. ṇihaṇaṁ kūlaṇ. ṇigaḍhō gharmaḥ. ṇisuaṁ tathā ṇisāmiaṁ śrutam. yathā–

ṇisuē ṇirulīrāvē ṇisāmiē saüṇikalayalē a vahū |

ṇaïṇihaṇāgayajāraṁ muṇia ṇiukkāhisaraï ṇigaḍhē vi || 27 || [ 27 ]

ṇiurammi ṇialamavisēsiammi ṇiriaṁ ca ṇikkhuḍamakampē |

ṇivvēḍhaṇivvaḍhā ṇaggē ṇijjūhō a ṇivvammi || 28 ||

ṇialaṁ nūpuram. ṇiriaṁ aviśēṣitam. ṇikkhuḍaṁ akampam. ṇivvēḍhō tathā ṇivvaḍhō nagnaḥ. ṇijjūhō nīvram. yathā–

ṇiriaṭṭhāṇāṭhāṇaya kiṁ ṇialē ṇiasi ṇikkhuḍō cōra |

jaraṇijjūhammi gharē ṇivvēḍhō ṇivvaḍhēṇa pēlliaï || 28 || [ 28 ]

aribhavaṇammi ṇiāraṁ ṇivvūḍhaṁ pacchimaṅgaṇaē |

kaḍhiṇammi ṇikkaḍaṁ taha ṇipphēsō saddaṇiggamaṇē || 29||

ṇiāraṁ ripugr̥ham. ṇivvūḍhaṁ gr̥hapaścimāṅganam. ṇikkaḍaṁ kaṭhinam. ṇipphēsō śabdanirgamaḥ. yathā–

dhaṇukaḍḍhaṇaṇikkaḍabhua cālukka tuhaṁ ṇiāraṇivvūḍhē |

ṇīsaṅkavilasirāṇaṁ sivāṇa ullasaï ṇipphēsō || 29 || [ 29 ]

ṇaṭṭhammi ṇirādō ṇicchiē ṇiruttaṁ ṇaē ṇiriṅkō a |

santuṭṭhammi ṇisattō vi ṇimēlaṁ dantamaṁsammi || 30||

ṇirādō naṣṭaḥ. ṇiruttaṁ niścitam. ṇiriṅkō nataḥ. ṇisattō santuṣṭaḥ. ṇi mēlaṁ dantamāṁsam. ṇimēlā iti dhanapālaḥ. yathā–

tuha ghāyaṇimēlucchuḍḍadantayā riugayā ṇiriṅkamuhā |

janti ṇirādā taha vi hu jaē ṇiruttaṁ tumaṁ si ṇa ṇisattō || 30 || [ 30 ]

ṇillaṅkaṇilaṅkā paḍigahammi ṇijjōbhiṇōmiṇō rassī |

aṅguṭṭhīi ṇiraṅgīṇīraṅgīu ahiammi ṇippaṭṭhō || 31 ||

ṇillaṅkō tathā ṇilaṅkō patadrahaḥ. ṇijjōmī tathā ṇōmī raś‍miḥ. rajjuri tyarthaḥ. ṇiraṅgī tathā ṇīraṅgī śirō 'vaguṇṭhanam. ṇippaṭṭhō adhikaḥ. yathā–

ṇijjōmikhañciōsaharahaōiṇṇē piammi lēi vahū |

ṇippaṭṭhapēmmaviraïaṇiraṅgiā karayaṇillaṅkē || 31 ||

kiṁ māmi rōasi tumaṁ ṇīraṅgiṁ caïa ācama ṇilaṅkē |

pēkkhasi ṇa cirā daïaṁ ṇōmībaddhaṁ purō baïllaṁ va || 32 || [ 31 ]

ṇimmaṁsū taruṇē ṇibbhuggō bhaggammi ṇikkhayaṁ ṇihaē |

suttōṭṭhiammi ṇivvittō ṇissaṅkō a ṇibbharaē || 32 ||

ṇimmaṁsū taruṇaḥ. ṇibbhuggō bhagnaḥ. ṇikkhayaṁ nihatam. ṇivvittō sup‍tō tthitaḥ. ṇissaṅkō nirbharaḥ. yathā–

ṇissaṅkakāmasaraṇikkhayā imā siviṇaē tumaṁ daṭṭhuṁ |

ṇimmaṁsua ṇivvittā ṇibbhuggamaṇōrahā hōi || 33 || [ 32 ]

ṇijjōō payarē parihiē ṇiatthaṁ calammi ṇikkajjō |

ṇivvāṇaṁ duhakahaṇē thaḍḍhē ṇiṭṭhūhaṇivvūḍhā || 33 ||

ṇijjōō prakaraḥ. puṣpāvakara ity anyē. ṇiatthaṁ parihitam. ṇikkajjō anavasthitaḥ. ṇivvāṇaṁ duḥkhakathanam. ṇiṭṭhūhō tathā ṇivvūḍhō stabdhaḥ. yathā–

ṇikkajjē jaṁ maṇṇasi ṇiatthahāraṁ phuliṅgaṇijjōaṁ |

ṇiṭṭhūhē ṇivvāṇaṁ kuṇasu aṇivvūḍhayāṇaṁ ta amha || 34 || [ 33 ]

gayakusalōvakiīsuṁ ṇimmayaṇigghaṭṭhaṇijjāyā |

sēdōciaüjjāṇā ṇivāyaṇivviṭṭhaṇibbhaggā || 34 ||

ṇimmaō gataḥ. ṇigghaṭṭhō kuśalaḥ. ṇijjāō upakāraḥ. ṇivāō svēdaḥ. ṇivviṭṭhaṁ ucitam. upabhuktārthaṁ tu nirviṣṭaśabda-bhavam. ṇibbhaggaṁ udyānam. yathā–

ṇibbhaggaṇimmayaṁ taṁ daṭṭhuṁ payaḍiāṇivāyasiḍhilaṅgī |

tammaï tujjha kaē ṇivviṭṭhaṇijjāyaṇigghaṭṭhaय़ || 35 || [ 34 ]

suttapasuttammi ṇisāyaṁ cāmuṇḍāi ṇimmaṁsā |

ṇiddhammō ēgamuhammi ṇindiṇiṇiāṇiā kutiṇaharaṇē || 35 ||

ṇisāyaṁ suptaprasuptam. caṇḍālavācakas tu ṇisāyaśabdō niṣādaśabda-bhavaḥ. ṇi mmaṁsā cāmuṇḍā. ṇiddhammō ēkamukhayāyī. ṇindiṇī tathā ṇiāṇiā kutr̥ṇō ddharaṇam. yathā–

kēāraṇindiṇikaē ṇiāṇiāmullajampaṇamisēṇa |

ṇimmaṁsadēulaṁ ṇiddhamma piā vaccaï ṇisāē || 36 || [ 35 ]

ṇiṇṇālā ṇōlacchā ṇōlaïā cēa cañcubhmi |

ṇiggiṇṇaṁ ṇillasiaṁ ca ṇiggaē pāḍiē ṇisuddhaṁ ca || 36 ||

ṇiṇṇālā tathā ṇōlacchā tathā ṇōlaïā cañcuḥ. ṇiggiṇṇaṁ tathā ṇillasiaṁ nirgatam. ṇisuddhaṁ pātitam. yathā–

ṇōlaïāi haṇantō ṇōlacchivarō visālaṇisālō |

ṇiggiṇṇajiō hūō āsamaṇillasiarāvaṇaṇisuddhō || 37 || [ 36 ]

ṇijjhāō ṇicchuṇḍō ṇirāhaṇigghōraṇippharisā |

ṇiddhandhasō a ṇivvērisō a adaē ṇimēṇamavi ṭhāṇē || 37 ||

ṇijjhāyādayaḥ sapta śabdā nirdayavācakāḥ. ṇivvērisaśabdō ’tyarthē ’pi dr̥śyatē. ṇimēṇaṁ sthānam. yathā–

ṇigghōrē ṇicchuṇḍō aṇirāhē kō vva ṇa hu aṇippharisō |

ṇiddhandhasē aṇivvērisō aṇijjhāya kattha vi ṇimēṇē || 38 || [37]

avibhiṇṇagēhaē ṇiddhamaṇiddhayaṇiddhamāyā vi |

ṇiaraṭṭhiē ṇiariaṁ ṇiandhaṇaṇiaṁsaṇā vatthē || 38 ||

ṇiddhamō tathā ṇiddhaō tathā ṇiddhamāō avibhinnagr̥haḥ. atra. ṇiaï paśya ti. ṇivvāi viśrāmyati. ṇimaï nyasyati. ētē dhātvādēśēṣūktā iti nōktāḥ. ṇiariaṁ nikarēṇa sthitam. ṇiandhaṇaṁ tathā ṇiaṁsaṇaṁ vastram. yathā–

ṇiariaguṇa suṇiaṁsaṇa ṇiandhaṇaṁ kaḍḍha ṇiddhamō havia |

ṇiddhaa vayammi ramimō kiṁ pēmmamaṇiddhamāyāṇa || 39 || [38]

ṇiddhamaṇaṁ ōghasarē ṇiakkalaṁ vaṭṭulē cēa |

ṇivvamiaṁ parihuttē pāṇiggahaṇāmmi ṇivvahaṇaṁ || 39 ||

ṇiddhamaṇaṁ gr̥hajalapravāhaḥ. ṇiakkalaṁ vartulam. ṇivvamiaṁ paribhuktam. ṇivvahaṇaṁ vivāhaḥ. yathā–

gandhavvē ṇivvahaṇē tuha ṇivvamiaṁ ṇiakkalathaṇīē |

virahē sumarantīē bāhēhiṁ vahaï ṇiddhamaṇaṁ || 40 || [39]

adaḍhammi a ṇikkhuriaṁ ṇirantarē cēa ṇittiraḍī |

ōāraṇē ṇivacchaṇaṇēvacchaṇayā cuammi ṇissariaṁ || 40 ||

ṇikkhuriaṁ adr̥ḍham. ṇittiraḍī nirantaram. ṇivacchaṇaṁ tathā ṇēvacchaṇaṁ ava tāraṇam. ṇissariaṁ srastam. yathā–

ṇittiraḍivirahaṇikkhuriataṇū ṇissaria aṁsu pattapiē |

ṇēvacchaṇagahakhaliā sayamēva ṇivacchaṇīhuā vahuā || 41 ||

atra. ṇiacchaï paśyati. ṇirappaï tiṣṭhati. ṇimmāṇaï ṇimmavaï nirmi mītē. ṇijjharaï kṣīyatē. ṇihuvaï kāmayatē. ṇiāraï kāṇēkṣitaṁ karōti. ṇirigghaï nilīyatē. ṇivvaḍaï pr̥thak spaṣṭō vā bhavati. ṇiṭṭhuhaï niṣṭambhaṁ karōti. ṇivvōlaï manyunōṣṭhaṁ malinaṁ karōti. ṇilluñchaï muñcati. ṇiuḍḍaï majjati. ṇicchallaï ṇijjhōḍaï ṇillūraï chinatti. ṇisuḍhaï bhārākrāntō namati. ṇiḍḍuaï kṣarati. ṇiṭṭuhaï vigalati. ṇimmahaï gacchati. ṇillasaï ullasati. ētē dhātvā dēśēṣūktā iti nōktāḥ || [40]

ṇiṭṭhuhiaṇikkhasariaṇiruvakkayā thukkamusiaakaēsu |

ṇittiraḍiaṁ ca tuṭṭē ṇīsārō maṇḍavē cēa || 41 ||

ṇiṭṭhuhiaṁ thūtkr̥tam. niṣṭhyūtamityarthaḥ. ṇikkhasariō muṣitaḥ. apahr̥tasāra iti yāvat. ṇiruvakkayaṁ akr̥tam. ṇittiraḍiaṁ truṭitam. atra. ṇiruvāraï gr̥hṇāti. ṇiriṇajjaï pinaṣṭi. ityētau dhātvādēśēṣūktāviti nōktau. ṇīsārō maṇḍapaḥ. yathā–

tuha ṇittiraḍiathāmā riuṇō ṇikkhasariā vasanti vaṇē |

ṇiruvakkayaṇīsārē taṇhāi susantaṇiṭṭhuhiā || 42 || [41]

ṇīsampāyaṁ parisantajaṇavaē taha jhuṇimmi ṇīhariaṁ |

ṇīsīmiō a ṇivvāsiammi bāṇammi ṇīlakaṇṭhī a || 42 ||

ṇīsampāyaṁ pariśrāntajanapadam. ṇīhariaṁ śabdaḥ. ṇīsīmiō nirvāsitaḥ. ṇīlakaṇṭhī bāṇavr̥kṣaḥ. yathā–

vōliavahū ṇisamuhaṁ ṇīsampāē aṇīhariakañcī |

ahisaraï ṇīlakaṇṭhīvaṇammi ṇīsīmiassa tassa kaē || 43 || [42]

ṇīsaṇiā ṇissēṇī ṇīāraṇamavi balighaḍīē |

ṇūlā sāhāē paṭṭavāsiāē a ṇēḍālī || 43 ||

ṇīsaṇiā niḥśrēṇī. kapratyayābhāvē ṇīsaṇītyapi. ṇīāraṇaṁ balighaṭī. atra. ṇīi ṇīṇaï ṇīlukkaï gacchati. ṇīrañjaï bhanakti. ṇuvvaï prakāśayati. ētē dhātvādēśēṣūktā iti nōktāḥ. ṇīhammiaṁ nirgatam ititu nirpūrvasya hammi dhātōḥ siddham. ṇūlā śākhā. atra ṇūmaï chādayatīti dhātvādēśēṣūktamiti nōktam. ṇēḍālī paṭṭavāsitā. śirōbhūṣaṇabhēdaḥ. yathā–

ṇēḍālisundara tumaṁ puttaya mā caḍasu uccataruṇūlaṁ |

jaṁ ṇīsaṇipaḍiēsu vi ṇīāraṇavallahā ṇa hōi chalaṁ || 44 || [43]

ṇēuḍḍō sabbhāvē kūvatulāē a ṇēlicchī |

ravivaṇiasacivasaṇḍhā ṇēsaraṇēsatthiṇēlacchā || 44 ||

ṇēuḍḍō sadbhāvaḥ. ṇēlicchī kūpatulā. ṇēsarō raviḥ. ṇēsatthī vaṇiksa civaḥ. ṇēlacchō ṣaṇḍhaḥ. vr̥ṣabha ity anyē. yathā–

ṇēsatthi aṇēlacchō taṁ ṇēuḍḍēṇa ṇēsaratthamaṇē |

ṇēlicchiravaṁ sōuṁ vaccaï jaṁ jalamisēṇa tuha jāyā || 45 ||

atra ṇēḍḍaṁ nīḍam ititu nīḍaśabda-bhavam itinōktam || [44]

bhaddavaōjjaladasamīūsavabhēammi ṇēḍḍariā |

ucchuṇivīḍaṇakaṇḍē tahēa kuṇḍammi ṇandaṁ ca || 45 ||

ṇēḍḍariā bhādrapadōjjvaladaśamyāṁ kaścidutsavaviśēṣaḥ. yathā–

saṅkēamāgaē uvavaïmmi dūīi jhatti saṁlaviā |

ahisaraï ṇāyaravahū ṇēḍḍariādaṁsaṇamisēṇa || 46 ||

atra ṇōllaï kṣipatīti dhātvādēśēṣūktam itinōktam.

ṇandaṁ ikṣunipīḍanakāṇḍaṁ kuṇḍākhyō bhāṇḍaviśēṣaś cēti dvyartham. kēcittu. ikṣunipī ḍanakāṇḍavācakāvēva ṇandakuṇḍaśabdaudēśyāvityāhuḥ. yad āha— || ikṣunipīḍanakāṇḍaṁ ṇandaṁ kuṇḍaṁ ca gō ṇandī || na tu kuṇḍākhyabhāṇḍavācī ṇandaśabdō dēśyaḥ. asmābhi stūbhayamapi dr̥ṣṭamityanēkārthēṣūpanibaddham || [45]

ghāṇē mūkē ṇakkō ṇaṇṇō kūvē khalaggajēsuṁ ca |

kaddamiē vaïvivarē paōaṇē ṇallayaṁ ṇimittē a || 46 ||

ṇakkō ghrāṇaṁ mūkaś ca. grāhē tu ṇakkaśabdō nakraśabda-bhava ēva. ṇaṇṇō kūpō durjanō jyēṣṭhō bhrātā cēti tryarthaḥ. ṇallayaṁ kardamitaṁ vr̥tivivaraṁ prayōjanaṁ nimittaṁ cēti caturartham || [46]

rayaduddiṇēsu ṇaḍḍalamaha ṇaddhambavayamaghiṇaṇindāsu |

sabbhāvē ’bhippāē ṇāuḍḍō cōrakañcaṇē ṇikkhō || 47 ||

ṇaḍḍalaṁ rataṁ durdinaṁ ca. ṇaddhambavayaṁ aghr̥ṇā nindā cēti dvyartham. ṇāuḍḍō sadbhāvō ’bhiprāyaś ca. manōratha ity anyē. ṇikkhō cōraḥ kāñcanaṁ ca || [47]

kaühachaümēsu ṇivvaṁ ṇiayaṁ rayasayaṇasāsayaghaḍēsu |

suttōṭṭhiē ṇirāsē ubbhaḍaakivēsu a ṇividdhō || 48 ||

ṇivvaṁ kakudaṁ vyājaś ca. paṭalāntē tu ṇivvaśabdō nīvraśabda-bhava ēva. ṇiayaṁ rataṁ śayanīyaṁ śāśvataṁ ghaṭaś cēti caturartham. ṇividdhō suptōtthitō nirāśa udbhaṭō nr̥śaṁsaś cēti caturarthaḥ || [48]

sēagaṇēsu ṇihāō puṭṭhē uvvēḍhiē ṇirappō a |

cōraṭṭhiapuṭṭhēsuṁ ṇirakkamujjuadaḍhēsu ṇippicchaṁ || 49 ||

ṇihāō svēdaḥ samūhaś ca. ṇirappō pr̥ṣṭhamudvēṣṭitaṁ ca. ṇirakkō cōraḥ sthitaḥ pr̥ṣṭhaṁ cēti tryarthaḥ. ṇippicchaṁ r̥ju dr̥ḍhaṁ ca || [49]

payaḍōjjuriūsu ṇirāō ṇiṭṭaṅkaṁ ca ṭaṅkiē visamē |

ṇihuaṁ ṇivvāvārē tuṇhikkē taha ya surayammi || 50 ||

ṇirāō prakaṭa r̥jū ripuś cēti tryarthaḥ. ṇiṭṭaṅkaṁ ṭaṅkicchinnaṁ viṣamaṁ ca. ṇihuaṁ nirvyāpāraṁ tūṣṇīkaṁ surataṁ cēti tryartham. [50]

ṇivvaliaṁ jaladhōē pavigaṇiē vihaḍiē cēa |

vāyasamūkēsu ṇiukkaṇō ṇihēlaṇamagārajaghaṇēsu || 51 ||

ṇivvaliaṁ jaladhautaṁ pravigaṇitaṁ vighaṭitaṁ cēti tryartham. ṇivvalēi duḥkhaṁ muñcati niṣpadyatē kṣarati cēti dhātvādēśē siddham. ṇiukkaṇō vāyasō mūkaś ca. ṇihēlaṇaṁ gr̥haṁ jaghanaṁ ca. atra. ṇivvaraï duḥkhaṁ kathayati chinatti ca. ṇihōḍaï nivārayati pātayati ca. ṇilukkaï tuḍati nilīyatē ca. ṇivahaï ṇiriṇāsaï gacchati pinaṣṭi naśyati ca. ṇīluñchaï niṣpatati ācchōṭayati ca. ṇīravaï bubhukṣatē ākṣipati ca. ṇīharaï niḥsarati ākrandati ca. ṇumaï nyasyati chāda yati cēti dhātvādēśēṣūktā iti nōktāḥ || [51]

tambā gāī taṇṭaṁ puṭṭhaṁ suttōppalēsu taggataṇā |

taṭṭī vaīi sōgammi tamō tavaṇī a bhakkhammi || 1 ||

tambā gauḥ. taṇṭaṁ pr̥ṣṭham. taggaṁ sūtram. sūtram itisāmānyābhidhānē ’pi sūtrakaṅkaṇamucyatē. yad āha— || taggaṁ ca sūtrakaṅkaṇakam || taṇaṁ utpalam. taṭṭī vr̥tiḥ. tamō śōkaḥ. tavaṇī bhakṣaṇayōgyam. kaṇādi. yathā–

taṇṭavahaṇataṭṭivihīhi tambacāraṇaya taggavalaṇahi |

taṇalōaṇā ṇa tavaṇiṁ kuṇanti virahē tamaṁ jaḍā janti || 1 || [1]

tamaṇaṁ cullī taharī bahalasurā vāvaḍē tavaō |

tasiaṁ sukkē sayaṇē tallaḍamōllammi taṇṇāyaṁ || 2 ||

tamaṇaṁ culliḥ. taharī paṅkilā surā. tavaō vyāpr̥taḥ. tasiaṁ śuṣkam. tallaḍaṁ śayyā. taṇṇāyaṁ ārdram. yathā–

virahammi tujjha sūhava tasiē taṇṇāyakamalatallaḍaē |

tamaṇaṁ va tappaï sahī taharītavaō ṇa jāṇasi tumaṁ tu || 2 || [2]

tacchiṇḍaṁ ca karālē ṇayarārakkhē talārō a |

tattillō tallicchō a tapparē taṇacaē taṇēsī a || 3 ||

tacchiṇḍaṁ karālam. talārō nagarārakṣakaḥ. tattillō tathā tallicchō tatparaḥ. taṇēsī tr̥ṇaprakaraḥ. yathā–

dōsagavēsaṇatattilla talārabhayā taṇēsiantariā |

ua taï tallicchā sā tamatacchiṇḍē paḍicchaï kuḍaṅgē || 3 || [3]

tarasaṁ maṁsē tambēhitambaṭakkāriāu sēhālī |

icchāi takkaṇā tantaḍitōntaḍiā karambammi || 4 ||

tarasaṁ māṁsam. tambēhī tathā tambaṭakkārī śēphālikā. takkaṇā icchā. tantaḍī tathā tōntaḍī karambaḥ. yathā–

caya tambēhikuḍaṅgaṁ ṇa tambaṭakkārirattavasaṇō ’aṁ |

ṇa hu tarasatakkaṇaṁ kaṅgutantaḍī kalamatōntaḍī a harē || 4 || [4]

gōhumakuṅkumiāē a tambirā tambarattī a |

taravaṭṭō paümāḍammi taḍavaḍā āulitarummi || 5 ||

tambirā tathā tambarattī gōdhūmēṣu kuṅkumacchāyā. taravaṭṭō prapunāṭaḥ. taḍavaḍā āulivr̥kṣaḥ. yathā–

sahi tambarattirammē chēttē suttammi tambiracchi piē |

taravaṭṭataḍavaḍāulakuḍaṅgaē kīsa caliā si || 5 ||

atra. taliṇaṁ sūkṣmam ititalinaśabda-bhavam. taraï śaknōti. tacchaï takṣṇō ti. taḍaï taḍḍaï taḍḍavaï tanōti. ētē dhātvādēśēṣūktā iti nōktāḥ || [5]

indōvē tambakimī taṇasōllī malliāē a |

surayammi tattuḍillaṁ pasāriē cēa taṇarāsī || 6 ||

tambakimī indragōpaḥ. taṇasōllī mallikā. tattuḍillaṁ suratam. taṇarāsī prasāritam. yathā–

jaï tattuḍillapaṇḍia taṇasōllīvallahō gaō kālō |

tuha virahē taṇarāsiatambakimī pāusō kahaṁ tīē || 6 || [6]

sālimmi talapphalatālahalā khuhiē taḍamaḍō a |

tantukkhōḍī a turī uḍuvē tariavvataṇavaraṇḍīō || 7 ||

talapphalō tathā tālahalō śāliḥ. taḍamaḍō kṣubhitaḥ. tantukkhōḍī vāyakata ntrōpakaraṇam. tariavvaṁ tathā taṇavaraṇḍī uḍupaḥ. yathā–

kīsa talapphalagōvītaḍamaḍiō jāsi tālahalachēttaṁ |

tantukkhōḍia vaccasu tariavvaṇiutta taṇavaraṇḍīē || 7 || [7]

taddiasaṁ aṇudiasē tahalliā cēa gōvāḍē |

taddiacayaṁ ca ṇaccē talaāgattī a kūvammi || 8 ||

taddiasaṁ. adūraviprakarṣāt taddiasiaṁ. taddiahaṁ ity api. anudivasam. tahalliā gōvāṭaḥ. taddiacayaṁ nr̥tyam. talaāgattī kūpaḥ. yathā–

taruṇatahalliarakkhaya bhumayātaddiacaēṇa taddiasaṁ |

talaāgattiṁ vaccaï ṇisi vahuā pāṇiamisēṇa || 8 || [8]

taḍaphaḍiaṁ paricaliammi kuravaē tambakusumō a |
